Neutrality towards Spain; Britain and France Establish Agreement; Effective Upon Participation of All Countries; Britain Also Assists France in Urging Italy for a Response 19

(London) Yesterday afternoon, Britain and France finalized the full text of the agreement on France's proposal of non-intervention in Spain. The two governments exchanged notes in Paris as proof. The agreement will take effect after Germany, Italy, Portugal, and Russia respond with their approval. It is reported that the Soviet government is quite supportive. The Portuguese authorities have accepted it in principle. Germany and Italy have not yet made a final response. The British government is now assisting the French government in urging Rome for a response. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

(Paris) The British government has accepted the draft agreement on non-intervention in the Spanish civil war proposed by France. Sir Eric Phipps, the British Ambassador to France, submitted the formal reply of his government to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs this afternoon, stating that the agreement will take effect immediately after the governments of Germany, Italy, the Soviet Union, and Portugal agree to participate. Political figures here have expressed great satisfaction with Britain's decision, saying that Russia and Portugal have already submitted replies expressing their support for the French proposal. Therefore, the reference to the "governments of the four countries" in the British reply is directed at Germany and Italy, containing a direct appeal to the two countries. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

(London) The Foreign Office issued a public statement this evening, stating that "Regarding the original draft agreement on non-intervention proposed by France, which advocates that all signatory countries should not sell various munitions, military and civilian aircraft, and various warships to Spain or Spanish Morocco, Britain and France have now fully reached an agreement. The two governments exchanged notes in Paris this afternoon. This agreement will take effect immediately after the governments of Germany, Italy, the Soviet Union, and Portugal agree to participate." It is now learned that the Soviet government has expressed its support for this agreement, and the Portuguese government has also accepted the principle of non-intervention. However, Germany and Italy have not yet submitted a final response. The French government is currently in contact with Italy, and the British government is providing strong support to facilitate its success. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

(Paris) After the British government formally replied expressing its support for the draft agreement on non-intervention proposed by France, Britain and France have thus reached an agreement. The newspapers here commented on this matter, hoping that Germany and Italy would change their attitude so that the non-intervention agreement could be realized as soon as possible. "Le Journal" published a dispatch from its Berlin correspondent, claiming that the German reply was ready and that its content expressed agreement with the French draft. However, according to a telegram from the "Le Matin" in Berlin, the German government has decided not to respond to the French proposal for the time being. The extreme right-wing "Deutsche Tageszeitung" adopted the views of the Italian newspapers, saying that "The reason why the proposal put forward by France has failed to achieve the expected results is that, although this proposal sounds very appealing on the surface, when one examines its substance, some of the actions that our country's authorities should be directly responsible for are obviously contradictory to their statements. For example, the number of domestic donations for the Spanish Red Army is increasing, and communist members continue to enlist and go to Spain to join the military. Some cabinet members even openly support one of the two warring factions in Spain. All these situations are clear to everyone, and Britain, Germany, and Italy are all aware of them." The newspaper concluded by saying that the Secretary-General of the Unified Trade Union, Shi Wu, flew to Pasaia Port in Spain yesterday, and the purpose of this is difficult to understand. Gairnu, Chairman of the Left-wing Human Rights League, wrote an article in "Le Petit Journal" attacking domestic right-wing figures, saying, "They always talk about respecting justice and the law, but they praise the Spanish rebels who launched a coup to overthrow the legitimate government, which is self-contradictory. The reason why they adopt this attitude is largely because they hate the democratic system." Other newspapers, such as "L'Intransigeant", expressed concern about the recruitment of soldiers by the Spanish revolutionary army in French Morocco, saying that the French government must stop it. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

(Washington) The Colombian government has requested the State Department to allow the country's ministers and consuls in Spain to take refuge in the U.S. Embassy in Madrid. The State Department has accepted the request and has instructed the embassy in Spain to comply. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Lamenting the Spanish Battlefield: Cruelty Exceeds Ancient Times; Charging and Melee Fighting Bolder Than Personal Fights; Rebels Massacred More Than Two Thousand People; Orphans and Widows Search Through Piles of Corpses 20

Lisbon. The city of Badajoz, Spain, after fierce fighting between the two armies, was occupied by the rebel army on Friday evening. The truth about the destruction and terror within has been detailed to our agency today by a Portuguese reporter. This is the first journalist to enter the city after its fall. It is said that the rebel army commander who allowed him to enter the city warned him that this trip was extremely dangerous and instructed him to pay special attention to the seven Moorish troops patrolling the streets, as these soldiers were still very excited. The reporter also said that the undamaged parts of Badajoz were in a state of chaos. Every street was filled with obstacles. In fact, almost every obstacle was a pile of corpses. The walls in front of the military headquarters were splattered with blood, and bullet holes were as dense as a beehive. This is the trace of the more than two thousand people killed by the rebel army. When the reporter spoke with Colonel Yiyi, who is currently ruling Badajoz, he mentioned that more than two thousand people had been executed. Yiyi actually said, "What you said is very good, but the number of people killed may not be so many." It is said that women are often seen searching for their husbands and children in the piles of corpses in the streets, a situation that could not be more tragic. These orphans and widows are truly pitiful creatures in this barbaric civil war. According to a Spanish captain, the fall of Badajoz was due to a simultaneous attack from both sides. The battle lasted for forty-eight hours. When the Red Army fought, they were as brave as lions. Each army charged with bayonets, and their bravery was unprecedented since the formation of the militia. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

Elvas, Portugal. After the city of Badajoz, Spain, was occupied by the revolutionary army of that country a few days ago, our reporter made a special trip to inspect it. The city of Badajoz is the capital of the province of Badajoz, a famous fortress. The province of Badajoz is the largest province in Spain's fifty-one provinces. The railway from the capital Madrid to Lisbon, Portugal, passes through it. The population is dense, and the area is prosperous. As soon as the reporter entered the city yesterday, he saw blood splattered all over the streets. The magnificent bullring and all public buildings have been reduced to rubble. The desolation is like the sky from the earth compared to the past. According to military figures, since the revolutionary army entered the city, hundreds of Marxists have been shot. The captured left-wing workers were all lined up against the walls of the city's cathedral and shot. The reporter saw piles of corpses at the foot of the wall, and there were also two next to the altar. However, the church was not damaged. More than three hundred right-wing figures in the prisons were released. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

Slaughter Intensifies: The War Cannot End Immediately; No Major Changes Yesterday 21

(London) According to news from Spain, the rebellion has been going on for four weeks, and the slaughter is terrible, but there is still no hope of ending it. The rebels claim that the two headquarters in Burgos and Seville have been connected by railway and that the repairs of one battleship, two cruisers, and two light cruisers have been completed. The government claims that the rebels' offensive against Irun collapsed completely after six hours of fierce fighting. Several sailors died when the government warship "Jaime Primero" was bombed by the rebels a few days ago. When they were buried in Malaga yesterday, a rebel plane suddenly appeared in the sky, and the pallbearers fled in all directions. It is heard that President Azaña has ordered the cancellation of the suspension of convertibility, but any transactions with banks in the towns occupied by the rebels will be regarded as illegal. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

Madrid. There were no changes in the battle situation today. There were no major battles on the front lines. After the government forces recovered the city of Pozoblanco in the province of Córdoba, they are gradually advancing towards the city of Córdoba. Their columns in the province of Granada have also reached a village seven kilometers north of the city of Granada. The city of Oviedo, occupied by the rebels in the north, is still heavily surrounded by the Asturian miners' militia. President Azaña recently ordered that the rebel cruisers "España" and "Velasco" be declared pirate ships, and anyone who sees them should immediately bombard them without leniency. The Standing Committee of the House of Representatives recently decided to extend the "state of alert" for one month. General Fuhuer, a military officer who was dismissed on the 22nd of last month for supporting the rebellion, was brought to trial today. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Bayonne, France. According to news received at the border between France and Spain, government forces near San Sebastian have engaged in battle with the rebel army. As of the time of the telegram, the battle was fierce, and it was impossible to know who would win. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

Bayonne, France. It is learned here that a squadron of Spanish rebel warships, assisted by six bombers, launched a fierce attack on the port of San Sebastian today. At the same time, the army also attacked from the south. After a fierce melee, they have captured many places in their destination. According to refugees who fled the city, the city is likely to fall today. (National Telegram on the 15th)

Bayonne, France. It is learned here that the Spanish rebel army occupied the port of San Sebastian today after attacking from the sea, land, and air. (National Telegram on the 15th)

Burgos. Our correspondent reports exclusively that the government forces recently attacked the city of Navalmoral de la Mata, thirty kilometers west of Avila, west of the capital, but were defeated and suffered heavy losses. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Hendaye, France. A column of rebels in northern Spain attacked the city of Irun from the village of Oyarzun at dawn today and engaged in fierce fighting with the government forces defending the city in the surrounding area. The government forces initially retreated from the first line of defense. The rebels, believing they had won, chased after them. However, the government forces retreated to the second line of defense and immediately counterattacked. The two sides fought for a long time before stopping fighting in the afternoon. At 8:00 PM, the sound of artillery was heard again, and 500-600 government forces reoccupied the first line of defense. The rebels recaptured the village of Encinaschaya at 10:00 PM. More than fifty rebels were killed in the battle, and more than one hundred were injured. Many local residents fled across the border into France. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Seville. General Triana, commander of the Southern Route of the revolutionary army, issued a broadcast report yesterday, advising the miners in the Tinto River basin in the southern province of Huelva to assist the government forces in fighting, urging them to surrender immediately, saying that many towns and villages near the Tinto River have been occupied by our army, and I have detained seventy miners as hostages. I hope you will not forget. For your sake, the best thing to do is to surrender immediately. You must know that our army is constantly reporting victories and gaining the upper hand day by day. Moreover, the road from the city of Burgos in the north to this city has been reopened, which shows that our army has established contact between the north and south routes. The fall of the capital Madrid is not far away. The Marxists, in view of this, vainly hope to mobilize other countries to come out and mediate, so that they can prolong their lives, but they know that this is impossible. They only have one way to surrender unconditionally. There are rumors that I personally have ambitions, which is not true. This is what I want to state. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

Barcelona. The situation in Catalonia has returned to peace in recent days, and the people here are greatly relieved. All the theaters have reopened, and the audience is coming in droves, still like a tide. A soccer game and a bullfight will be held tomorrow, and the proceeds will be used to comfort the bereaved families of those who died in this anti-fascist war. The famous cellist Pablo Casals has also volunteered to hold concerts, often raising money to donate to hospitals and to comfort the wounded and dead soldiers. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Burgos. The rebels have occupied Bobadilla, the railway hub of Badajoz and the province of Andalusia. 1,500 people died in the battle of Badajoz. (National Telegram on the 15th)

British Three-Engine Aircraft Crashes on French Border; Rumored That Three Aircraft Flew to Spain 22

(London) It is said that three "Babylon" aircraft departed from Croydon Aerodrome and flew to Spain. Beforehand, representatives of the companies to which the aircraft belonged claimed that the aircraft were flying to Barcelona, Spain, but the pilots were not employees of the company. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Hendaye, France. A large Fokker three-engine aircraft crashed and fell to the ground near the Biarritz Aerodrome, and the fuselage was completely destroyed. Later, two skulls were found in the wreckage, both burned to charcoal. The origin of this aircraft is currently being investigated by the local authorities. Also, news came from La Rochelle that a similar large aircraft landed at La Coure Aerodrome with a slightly damaged right wing. The aircraft was registered in the UK, has sixteen seats, but no passengers. The pilot is Polish, and it is said that it was originally scheduled to fly to Portugal but could not continue due to fog. According to yesterday's "London Evening Standard", two large Fokker three-engine aircraft, each capable of carrying sixteen passengers, flew out of Croydon Aerodrome in London and headed for Burgos, Spain, likely the above-mentioned two aircraft. (Havas dispatch on the 15th)

Bayonne, France. A British three-engine large aircraft crashed near the Biarritz Aerodrome yesterday. The Polish pilot, Rosati, died on the spot, and his remains were burned to charcoal. The British Consul here has reported this matter to his country's government. Another British aircraft of the same type landed in La Rochelle. The pilot is also Polish. The local authorities investigated and decided to detain the aircraft and release the pilot. It is now known that this aircraft is one of the four British aircraft that recently flew to France and was detained by the local authorities in Bordeaux. After negotiations, it was allowed to fly back to the UK. Unexpectedly, it returned again within a few days. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

Biarritz, France. Last night, a Fokker aircraft, likely British, crashed and burned here. The passengers inside were all burned to ashes. The number of passengers is unknown because the fuselage was completely destroyed and the corpses are difficult to identify. The aerodrome here was not aware of the aircraft's arrival beforehand. Judging from the circumstances of its landing, the pilot seemed to have no experience. (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

(London) It is rumored here that several secret aircraft fly from England to Spain every day to join the government and rebel armies. Yesterday, four aircraft flew from Gatwick, and it was initially unknown where they were going. Later, it was learned that they were sold to Poland for commercial aviation purposes and had nothing to do with Spain. Also, six British aircraft are currently being detained by the authorities at the Le Perthus border crossing in France. When asked about them, they insisted, "We know nothing." (Reuters dispatch on the 16th)

An Italian Warship Another Arrives at Rebel Port; Story of Non-Intervention Agreement Delayed 23

Rabat, French Morocco. An Italian warship arrived in Cadiz, Spain this morning, stayed for a short time, and then took the route to Sanlúcar de Barrameda and sailed to Seville. (Havas dispatch on the 16th)

(Rome) Although officials here believe that the agreement on non-intervention in the Spanish civil war will eventually be reached, the Italian side does not seem to be eager to proceed with the negotiations initiated by the French government. Rebel Army Establishes Military Government 25

Burgos: After the National Military Government organized by the revolutionary army was established, it has been operating for many days. The following is a brief account of its organization and work: General Cabanellas was elected as Chairman, General Dávila as Minister of the Interior and concurrently Governor of Burgos. In military affairs, General Franco was appointed Commander of the Southern Route, General Mola Commander of the Northern Route, Colonel Gortron Chief of Staff, and General Saliquet Commander of the Seventh Division. General Ponte is stationed in Valladolid Province and commands the front lines of the Guadarrama Mountains and Somo Sierra Passes (north of Madrid). The military government has also established committees for finance, agriculture, transportation, and propaganda. In addition, committees have been established in the provinces occupied by the revolutionary army to take charge of the affairs of banks and various industrial and commercial groups. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Burgos: The National Military Government is now preparing various facilities and intends to issue orders to organize all occupations in the occupied areas into groups, and to control the capital and wages of workers in various industries. In addition, certain laws and rights enjoyed by local governments in various provinces that had been abolished by the central government have now been approved by the military government to be restored by the provincial councils. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

Rabat, French Morocco: The garrison stationed in Ifni, Spanish Africa, which has always been loyal to the government, suddenly revolted yesterday and immediately announced its support for the rebel leader General Franco. The commander, Montelo, was arrested and his fate is unknown. The Spanish government had just remitted 11 million pesetas (Spanish currency) from Madrid yesterday for military pay, which was intercepted by the garrison. As of now, the situation throughout Ifni remains calm. (Havas dispatch, 16th)

France Submits Amendment to League Covenant: Mutual Assistance Limited to Region 26

(Geneva) French Foreign Minister Delbos recently sent another document to League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, explaining the French government's views on the issue of amending the League Covenant, which can be roughly divided into three levels: (1) French Prime Minister Léon Blum and himself had previously made statements at the League of Nations General Assembly on July 1st and 3rd, reaffirming France's adherence to the collective security system, and now reiterated it. (2) The obligation of mutual assistance must be limited so that those who bear this obligation are limited to countries neighboring the invaded country. (3) Expand the authority of the League of Nations, but the main principles on which the Covenant is based and collective responsibility should not be reduced. In addition, Delbos also said that the French government is very willing to adjust Articles 11 and 16 of the Covenant. In other words, the measures stipulated in Article 11 of the Covenant do not need to be implemented through a unanimous vote of all members of the Executive Council, so that those who threaten peace will not be able to escape punishment due to a single vote. Regarding Article 16 of the Covenant, regional mutual assistance conventions should be concluded between countries with the same geographical location or common interests, so that the economic, financial and military sanctions contained in that article can be mutually reinforcing. The French government will submit more detailed and specific measures regarding the above viewpoints before the next League of Nations General Assembly convenes, if necessary. However, it does not intend to submit a detailed plan at this time, because more than a month has passed since France made the proposal, and most countries have not yet decided on their position. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

French Chief of Staff Continues Talks with Polish Inspector General and Visits Air Force 27

Warsaw: French Army Chief of Staff General Gamelin continued his talks with Army Inspector General, General Ryz-Smigly, this morning. Later, accompanied by Chief of Staff, General Stachiewicz, he visited the First Air Force Regiment at the Woklence airfield near Warsaw, and then went to the aircraft manufacturing plant and the Danblin Air Force training camp to inspect everything. Opposition figures have recently expressed the opinion that the Polish government should take advantage of General Gamelin's visit to choose between pro-German and pro-French policies. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Warsaw: Today is the anniversary of Poland's victory over Soviet Russia in 1920. All opposition parties in the country, especially the Peasant Party, held demonstrations to celebrate. The celebrations in Wiechislawice were particularly enthusiastic, with no fewer than 20,000 participants, because the mayor of the city, Witos, was the leader of the Peasant Party and was the Prime Minister of Poland when Poland defeated Russia in 1920. In addition, the National Democratic Party and the Christian Socialist Party also held demonstrations. Major cities across the country with troops stationed also held military parades, which were very lively. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

Warsaw: According to a report from the Free City of Danzig, the old barracks of the garrison in the city have always been rented out for residential use. The municipal government authorities suddenly issued an eviction order, requiring all residents to move out before October 1st, and new barracks will be built on vacant land nearby. (Havas dispatch, 15th)

6th Pacific Science Congress Opens, Discusses Maintaining Peace, Suggests Organizing Permanent Far East Committee, League of Nations Sends Official Representatives to Observe 29

Yosemite, California, USA: The Sixth Pacific Science Congress opened at 7:30 pm on the 15th at Yosemite National Park, California. Representatives from eleven countries gathered for the opening ceremony. After dinner, Chairman Weeks (former US Secretary of War) gave an opening speech, emphasizing the necessity for countries along the Pacific coast to strive to maintain world peace through mutual agreement. Howard, the director of the Pacific Affairs Research Association, gave a presentation on the topics of this conference. The meeting adjourned at 9:00 pm. The official meeting will be held for two weeks from the 16th at the Awani Hotel in the park. Representatives from various countries will begin heated discussions. (Allied Telegraph, 15th)

Yosemite, California, USA: The Pacific Science Congress opened here today. Representatives from countries along the North Pacific, such as China, Japan, the Philippines, Hawaii, Canada, Soviet Russia, and the United States, attended. Britain also participated in the meeting because it has various interests in the Pacific. Mexico did not send a representative. The delegations from various countries have a maximum of 35 people, all of whom are leaders in the domestic political, business, economic, and educational fields. The attendance of the Soviet Russian representatives for the first time is particularly important. The Soviet Union has always only participated in international organizations in Europe. This direct contact with the organization of Pacific countries shows that its interests in the Pacific have greatly increased. The League of Nations also sent officials to observe due to the importance of this conference. The person selected was Mr. Lennox, Director of the League of Nations Paris Office, who has already arrived here. Although the League of Nations does not participate in the opinions of all discussions and resolutions of the conference, Mr. Lennox's report will be a reference material for the League of Nations. The most important issues to be discussed at this conference are the following: (1) Suggesting an international organization to maintain peace in the Pacific; (2) Concluding a mutual assistance and non-aggression treaty between Pacific countries; (3) Organizing a permanent Far East Conference to prepare for consulting on various fixed emergency issues; (4) Establishing a border delimitation committee to handle all disputes regarding existing national borders by peaceful means. (National Telegraph, 15th)

U.S. Federal Reserve Raises Bank Reserve Requirements 31

(Washington) The Federal Reserve today implemented a 5% increase in bank reserve requirements in order to reduce credit expansion. Originally, banks were required to deposit one yuan with the reserve department for every twelve yuan received in deposits. This has now been changed to one yuan for every eight yuan in deposits. This will reduce credit expansion by 2.4 billion yuan. However, according to news from San Francisco, after the implementation of this regulation, someone has filed a lawsuit in the local court, requesting to prevent the Federal Reserve from increasing the reserve amount, on the grounds that the department's order is unconstitutional. (National Telegraph, 15th)

National Election Headquarters Explains Four Points 33

(Nanjing) Ling Zhang, the Chief Supervisor of Elections in Hunan Province, previously asked the General Office for an explanation of four points of doubt. The General Office has answered them: (1) Officials at all levels refer specifically to the heads of government offices at all levels. All officials at all levels may not be elected as representatives in the electoral district where they are located. (2) The Chairman of the Provincial Government, the heads of various departments and bureaus, the President of the High Court, and the Chief Prosecutor may not be elected as representatives in the province. (3) The commander of the security zone and the head of the team should be regarded as military and police officials. Members of party departments at all levels should not be treated the same as officials at all levels. Furthermore, inspectors in each district may not be elected in the district under their jurisdiction. The heads of the departments and bureaus under the county government and the heads of the sub-district offices may not be elected in the district under their jurisdiction. (Central News Agency Telegraph, 16th)

Anecdote of the Southern Tour: Current Situation of Remnant Bandits in Southern Zhejiang 40

— Special Correspondent of This Newspaper, Shi Ying

The border area of the four provinces of Zhejiang, Fujian, Jiangxi, and Anhui, comprising some thirty to forty counties, large and small, was once heavily tinged with red by Fang Zhimin's troops of the pseudo "Soviet Government of the Gan-Zhe-Min Province" in the past four or five years. Since the National Army's five encirclement and suppression campaigns, which forcibly drove Zhu De and Mao Zedong out of their so-called "Central Red Area" lair, the important towns in these four provinces were successively recovered. The general attention to the bandit suppression issue was mostly focused on the intelligence regarding Zhu and Mao's main forces fleeing westward to Sichuan and Guizhou and attacking northward into Shaanxi and Shanxi. The activities of the remnant bandits in these four provinces, as well as the effectiveness of their suppression, seemed like the setting sun, fleeting and not worth considering.

However, in reality, such optimism is not warranted. On the surface, the so-called "suppression of the remnant bandits" seems easier than suppressing the main forces, a task that can be accomplished quickly. But in reality, because the remnant bandits are all local natives, very familiar with the terrain and local customs, they disperse as civilians and gather as bandits. Their resistance capability is weak, but their mobility is stronger than that of the main forces. The troops tasked with suppressing these remnant bandits find that because they (the bandits) appear and disappear unpredictably, gathering and dispersing constantly, sending too many soldiers yields no target, and sending too few often leads to unexpected ambushes. Here is an analogy: killing a chicken certainly does not require a butcher's knife, but if the chicken is not a docile hen waiting to be slaughtered, but a wild chicken that flies and jumps, then not only will a "chicken knife" be useless, even a butcher's knife will have no place to be used. Therefore, the current military suppression of remnant bandits everywhere, coupled with the insufficient strength of the security forces and some of the National Army, even after a considerable period, has still not diminished the strength of the elusive remnant bandits. The external cause of this phenomenon is very similar to the aforementioned chicken-killing story.

Take the bandit situation in southern Zhejiang as an example. Since the National Army defeated Fang Zhimin's main force, it also transferred the 18th Army, victorious in the Jiangnan bandit suppression, to be stationed there. The bandit suppression military operations, sometimes intense and sometimes lax, have never ceased. During the recent unrest in Guangdong and Guangxi, the National Army was transferred to deal with it, giving the remnant bandits an opportunity of "when the cat is away, the mice will play." As a result, they began to stir, planning to rekindle the dying embers. The most obvious example is that Kaihua County was briefly lost last month, and at the beginning of this month, the villages were looted again. The bandits are now occupying Mount Dalong, organizing a county Soviet government, and are plotting to contact other bandit groups to advance into Changshan, Suian, and Qu County. On the eve of Kaihua's fall, Jiangshan received a phone call from Xiakou (60 li from Jiangshan City), only stating that three groups of bandits from northern Fujian, each with dozens of people, were attempting to attack Xiakou. Unexpectedly, the next morning, an alarm sounded, but it was a bandit force of 500 that had captured Kaihua. After the second looting of Kaihua's major villages, it was reported that "the bandit force had increased to more than 2,000, and the peasant bandits numbered up to 30,000. The security force shortened the defense line to protect the county seat." The bandits' surprise tactics and the ferocity of their red terror tactics are evident.

Tracing the history of the remnant bandits who have been roaming southern Zhejiang in recent years, it seems that they also have "no small background." After the pseudo 7th Army Group was defeated, a portion of it entered Zhejiang and was reorganized into the pseudo Independent Division, with Li Yu, former chief of staff of the 7th Army Group, as commander, and Liu Ying, former political commissar, remaining as political commissar. Recently, Huang Ligui, a barber by origin, was added. They are all notorious bandit leaders famous in three provinces. The pseudo Independent Division's organizational strength is divided into five columns, each column divided into three detachments, each detachment divided into three squads, each squad with seven or eight people. Each column has about one to two hundred people, over a hundred rifles, and one or two light and heavy machine guns and Mauser pistols. In addition, there are organizations such as peasant and worker guerrilla teams, whose numbers are difficult to estimate accurately. Their area of activity is no more than the border counties of Fujian, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi. Taking the southern Zhejiang area alone, it includes Kaihua, Suian, Changshan, Longyou, and Jiangshan counties, and sometimes extends to the Lishui area. Looking through local newspapers, one sometimes finds news of the same bandit leader carrying out a major looting on the same day in different neighboring provinces. This is not a newspaper misprint, but rather because the bandits' tracks are erratic and their actions are secretive, making them difficult to grasp.

The bandit army's tactics are based on guerrilla warfare, exploiting weaknesses and attacking unguarded areas, not fighting hard battles with the National Army. They often use small numbers of bandits to contain the actions of larger troop forces, such as placing guerrilla teams near the large army fortresses to operate, or moving large troop forces to distant rear areas to operate, always avoiding direct contact with the army. Whenever scouts arrive at a place, they establish communication stations and work networks, intelligence networks, etc., to maintain contact and supply from other sources. In the past, they also had wireless communication to exchange information, but it was later surrounded and confiscated by the army. Their economic sources usually rely on "attacking local bullies and extorting money from wealthy people." Bandit leaders such as Liu Ying and Huang Ligui always carry huge amounts of cash and silver. If bandit soldiers accumulate a lot of money, they must turn it over to the political commissar, otherwise they are considered reactionary and severely punished. They face many difficulties, and even food and winter clothing are often problematic. Wounded soldiers have no hospitals and can only be hidden in the homes of ordinary people for treatment. Some medicines are purchased directly from pharmacies (the owner of a large Western pharmacy in Qu County was killed for selling these medicines), and some are ordered from local bullies, who buy them and send them as a ransom. The most lacking is ammunition, so they often make great sacrifices to seize ammunition. Not long ago, a certain division had nine transport vehicles traveling from Jiangshan to Pucheng in northern Fujian. The bandits learned that the ninth vehicle was fully loaded with ammunition and planned to ambush it at a certain bridge. After the first eight vehicles passed, the bridge suddenly collapsed, and the ammunition carried by the remaining vehicle was completely unloaded and transported to the mountains. In addition, there are other sources of weapons, but most are related to unsavory dealings with other parties, which I will not elaborate on.

Their methods of communizing the people are that whenever they arrive in a place, they use existing group members, such as the Baojia system, schools, and the Green Gang, to induce the masses, or directly investigate the population, convene meetings, use the people's suffering to tell them to attack local bullies and distribute land, and proclaim that if they are unwilling to participate in red activities, they will not be given land in the future. Peasants see land as life, and some naturally willingly participate, especially ordinary paper workers who went on strike because the September 18th Incident lightly gave their product distribution markets of paper and ramie cloth in the Northeast to the enemy, thus these industries successively ceased, causing them to lose their jobs in large numbers and fall into a difficult life. When everyone was full of grief and at a loss, they suddenly heard the Communist Party's slogans of anti-imperialism and resistance against XX, which naturally more easily moved their heartstrings. If there are still hesitant farmers, they will also have the names of strong men listed, forced to be incorporated into the guerrillas. Those who do not work are executed for the crime of reaction. With such inducements and threats, why worry that party members will not gather more and more every day?

A friend named Wu Juefei, who came from northern Fujian, once served as an assistant to the special party department of a certain division in northern Fujian and as an instructor in the Zhenghe County Security Corps of the First Pacification Zone in Fujian. Although his official title was not large, his position was between the government and the people in the recovered areas, so he spoke of several practical materials related to this. The reporter believes that this is very valuable.

Mr. Wu said that the main reason why the remnant bandits in northern Fujian are difficult to eradicate is not on the bandit side, but on the official side. If politics are not clear and the government is not honest, then the "rampant" remnant bandits will not be completely eliminated. How many of those currently engaged in political work are not thinking about fiat money? Even if there are such people, it is difficult to guarantee that they will not be dragged "into the sea" by the bad environment. Take the county magistrate as an example. If he does not cooperate with the local gentry, firstly, he is afraid that they will find fault and cause trouble. A five-cent stamp can be used to accuse him to his superiors. Even if he is not removed from his post, he will have to shed a layer of skin. Secondly, it will not be easy to handle affairs. If the army is stationed and the county magistrate is ordered to conscript laborers, the county magistrate who does not have good relations with the local gentry will be at a loss. On the contrary, if he has good relations with the local gentry, they will help him pay for hiring laborers, allowing him to enjoy the benefits. However, afterwards, they will apportion the money to the common people for repayment, and you can only pretend to be mute. However, the common people should die.

He also said: The common people in northern Fujian are truly extremely poor. When I (Mr. Wu referring to himself) went to various places to guide the organization of the Baojia and train strong men, I was ordered by my superiors to collect a small fee of 20 cents per household from the people on the spot for the expenses required by each organization, and the extremely poor were exempt. However, the common people in the recovered areas and the neighboring bandit areas are all among the hungry, and who is not extremely poor? How can they be distinguished? To be exempt from taxation, everyone must be exempt. However, the imperial order is urgent, and there is no way to raise funds, so I had no choice but to collect the money. One family even sent six eggs prepared for the pregnant woman to eat, asking to use them as the price of 20 cents in fees (if the collection office allocates this substitute to the food expenses to make dishes, I don't know how to swallow it?). In some remote townships, they resist miscellaneous taxes and duties, and kill the collectors in groups. The government certainly cannot ignore it. As a result, unexpected social changes often occur. "The common people are very afraid of public officials, and public officials are also very afraid of the common people." This is truly an unprecedented miracle. If we try to calculate these unfortunate phenomena according to geometric algorithms, and apply the theorems of "officials force the people to rebel" and "the people are poor and become bandits" to calculate the result, then the question of whether the remnant bandits can be eliminated can be answered appropriately.

Mr. Yang's remarks can be called "experienced words" and can also be called "heartfelt words." Although this refers to northern Fujian, the various situations in southern Zhejiang, which is close at hand, are roughly the same. Therefore, I dare to borrow flowers to offer to the Buddha, summarizing Mr. Wu's conversation to make the conclusion of this article, "If the government reduces exploitation, the burden on the people is lighter, and the general hard-working masses all have a way to make a living, then it will be easier to completely eliminate the remnant bandits."

Dr. Locke Staley

Dr. Stuart Band

Taking Diogenes to Rome 55

— By Constance Coline, Translated by Yue Qi

(Taking Diogenes is an ancient Greek philosopher who often carried a lantern in the streets to seek the truth. – Translator's Note)

I recently visited Rome, where I spent two weeks trying to find a Fascist who could understand and was not biased. But I didn't even have the luck to run into just one.

I saw many enthusiastic supporters of Fascism. They are mindless practitioners who absorb spiritual nourishment from newspapers every day. These "core members" are satisfied with exaggerated rhetoric and lack the ability to judge the political and economic problems that endanger modern times, and keep saying "We are real, noble, smart, and brave." They form a class that seems to exist in any country, including the nobility, the bourgeoisie, and the common people. Rather than saying it is a social class, it is a class of intellect; in terms of physiognomy, we can say it belongs to the "muscular type."

I also met ideologues who explained to me that Fascism melts all parties in the furnace, making them into one party; they said that no one cares about his own private interests and dedicates himself to the public interest; they said that everyone feels happy in cities and villages; and they said that even if there are poor people, they don't suffer from poverty, because their "ideal" relieves them of their worries. I must admit that these ideologues really turned me upside down and really made me believe them. Unfortunately, the various facts I encountered proved that although they are all sincere, loyal, and believing people, their words are not reliable at all, because they have been stunned by their beliefs and lost any ability to recognize them.

In the end, I also felt that searching for the truth there made people very disappointed, because when we engage in such a search, we will realize that many of man's noblest illusions are based on incorrect interpretations.

For example:

A Fascist fanatic said: "The enthusiasm shown by the people when they donated wedding rings and gold jewelry to the motherland was completely sincere and really moving."

The evidence of the facts proves that in the days before the ceremony, counterfeit merchants made a fortune selling fake wedding rings.

Italian citizens living abroad all received individual pieces of mail from their home country, instructing them to send their gold jewelry to the nearby consulate.

Many Italians told me that they donated their wedding rings entirely out of fear, because if they disobeyed the order, they would suffer.

An ideologue said: The Party allows those who truly love the ideology to donate as much as they can afford. What is important is not their money but their beliefs.

The evidence of the facts proves that a poor woman without a husband or parents ran to the Party headquarters to renew her Party card. "Have you donated your wedding ring to the motherland?" they asked her. "I don't have a wedding ring." "Then your jewelry, or your crucifix?" "I don't have jewelry, and I don't have a crucifix. I have nothing." "Then you have to pay 100 lire, 80 lire more than usual, to replace the jewelry you should have donated."

She paid the full amount, because without a Party card, she would have absolutely no chance to find a job.

An ideologue said: The achievements of the cooperative system are admirable. Any worker is protected, and the interests of employers and workers are aligned. The cooperation between employers and employees has finally been realized.

The evidence of the facts proves that a civil engineering contractor (a Fascist Party member) said: "Since the adoption of the cooperative system, it has been difficult to hire good workers. They send workers to you, regardless of whether these workers are skilled or whether you are satisfied with them." I asked, "Do you think the cooperative system is improving?" He said, "It's all just officialdom. In general, it can be said that nothing has changed, because every time a reform comes, a plan to evade it is devised."

A Fascist fanatic said: Any Italian is prepared to die to protect the ideology.

The evidence of the facts proves that I personally know at least ten Italians who are prepared to die to overthrow the ideology.

On the political stage, I got to know another type of sincere supporter of the ideology. I thought their becoming Fascists was not out of necessity, and I also thought they were not deliberately concealing their feelings. I thought loving the ideology was the same as loving a lover: everyone is prone to misunderstand the source of love. From the time they participated in the activity, they closed the doors of critical consciousness and skeptical consciousness in their hearts.

But no matter how enthusiastic or how believing they are, I cannot regard them as "typical Fascists." What I have been looking for in these two weeks is an understanding and unbiased person who supports, loves, and adheres to the ideology entirely because of his own free will. But I could not find such a Fascist in the end.

Now let us turn to the enemies of Fascism and take a look. We can find all kinds of enemies of Fascism, but they are all not taken seriously. Of course, among them are the smartest, most chivalrous, and most educated Italians, but this fact is not important. Dictatorship does not need intelligence, does not need chivalry, and does not need culture; all it needs is obedience.

These people are not taken seriously because, in terms of class, they are individualists. They have no organization, and their opinions are inconsistent. They do not fit anywhere, they do not manipulate any actions, but people are afraid of them and avoid them, because being seen with them is bound to create a bad impression.

We must understand that the entire current Fascist organization is based on secret notifications. This type of notification creates fear, fear creates obedience, and almost nationwide slavery is thus accomplished. We must also understand that the reason why anti-Fascists are narrow-minded is the same as the reason why ideologues are narrow-minded. Listen to them speak, and you will think that their words are not reliable. They deny obvious truths, and they often agitate people's hearts in the same way as ideologues.

If we recall the chaotic state of Italy in 1922, we will understand why it was necessary to "do this." "This" has been done and done well. If they allowed newspapers to freely accept subsidies, freely criticize, and if any doubtful actions or discussions were not censored, would "this" have been done just as well? Probably not done just as well.

But now that Italy has passed through its adolescence crisis, the framework has been completed, and the plan has been implemented on time, why continue to bind this tamed beast? Why create new shackles like war that are supposed to be to save the people? Why prescribe more and more dangerous nationalistic goals for the people? Why make the people suffer material sacrifices? Probably not to make Fascism more important, nor to make it better. So, why?

I am reluctant to conclude that all of this is to preserve one person's power, but there are many times when I cannot help but think so.

(Translated from the Paris Political and Literary Monthly)

Page 10

Situation of the Western Banner Dispute: The Great Lama Attacks the Stone Prince's Residence; Fierce Fighting Near the Gegeqi Temple 56

——A Foreigner Commands the Army——

Baotou Dispatch: Shila Budorji of the Western Public Banner of the Urad League, due to his uncle, the Great Lama Yixi, and the former general of the banner, Gegeqi (in charge of all the banner's military power), Mantou, and others wanting to seize power from the Stone Prince, besieged the Prince's residence with troops in April of last year, causing disputes. Fierce battles occurred several times, lasting for months. The government dispatched personnel to mediate in various ways, and the matter was resolved in November of last year. The Stone Prince was suspended from his post for eight months according to an order from the Executive Yuan, while the Great Lama and others went to the Mongol Political Affairs Council in Bailing Temple. The Western Banner dispute was temporarily quelled. At the beginning of the incident, the Mongol Political Affairs Council sent a security team to Meiligeng Temple within the banner's territory. One of the conditions of the mediation was to order the team to withdraw to the temple. After the matter was settled, the team has remained stationed there without withdrawing. In early spring of this year, the Great Lama returned from the temple to Meiligeng Temple, gathering his old subordinates, planning to seize an opportunity to make trouble for the Stone Prince again. At the same time, a foreigner frequently traveled to and from Meiligeng Temple, secretly providing guidance, and an airfield was built there. Airplanes come and go from time to time, so Meiligeng Temple has now formed a special situation. Those in the know have long known that disputes will inevitably arise, and its significance is certainly different from the previous time. In July of this year, the Stone Prince's eight-month suspension period expired. Chairman Fu (Zuoyi) petitioned the Executive Yuan for his reinstatement. The Stone Prince returned to the banner a few days ago and resumed his position as co-Jasak. Unexpectedly, at the beginning of this month, the Great Lama suddenly led his followers to attack the Stone Prince's residence again. Upon receiving the news, the Stone Prince also deployed troops in Seden Hulutou Township (belonging to the Third District of Baotou) to prepare for defense. On the 6th of this month, the two sides opened fire in the township, and the fierce battle was quite intense. The Prince's army had fifty soldiers, and the Great Lama had more than seventy soldiers. Due to the disparity in numbers and the fact that the Great Lama's army had sophisticated weapons and ammunition, the Prince's army could not resist and retreated steadily. The Great Lama led his troops to pursue relentlessly. On the evening of the 9th, the Prince's army retreated to the vicinity of Gegeqi Temple and was caught up by the Great Lama. The two sides lined up in opposition for several hours. At dawn on the 10th, the battle resumed and was even more fierce. It continued until 5:00 PM without stopping. The Baotou County Government received a report from the Third District and urgently dispatched Yang Yingnan, the deputy director of the Security Department, by car to the Third District at around 7:00 AM on the 10th, in order to command the garrison security team to strictly guard the key crossings along the Yellow River, so as to prevent harassment of the residents of the county and maintain local security. It is said that Gegeqi Temple is located north of the Baotou-Wuwu highway, close to the highway. Since the 10th, automobiles have stopped running to avoid danger. It is also heard that there are four foreigners in the Great Lama's army, providing on-the-spot guidance.

Japanese Military Attaché Imai Talks: Bandit Disturbances in Eastern Sui Have Nothing to Do With Japan; Our Authorities Are Still Intensifying Precautions and Eliminating Disputes in the Western Public Banner 57

Beiping Dispatch: After the puppet army invading Eastern Sui was defeated, there have been no further actions recently. However, during this period, a dispute occurred in the Western Public Banner of Sui between the Great Lama Yi and the Stone Prince. The two sides have clashed multiple times since the 10th of this month. The outside world is concerned about this. According to sources, after a certain party's attempt to use puppet troops to invade Eastern Sui failed, they are now shifting their target to the Western Public Banner. The Western Public Banner, Suiyuan, and Baotou form a triangle, and the area is important. The Sui authorities, in view of this, are not only stepping up deployments for defense but are also making every effort to eliminate the disputes in the Western Public Banner.

When Japanese Embassy Military Attaché Imai Takeo met with Chinese and foreign reporters on the 14th, many inquired about the Eastern Sui issue. Imai said, "Regarding this issue, there have been many rumors from the outside world in recent days, but none of them are credible. The actual situation is that Chairman Fu (Zuoyi) of Suiyuan reportedly dispatched troops to Eastern Sui at the end of last month. Those who did not know the truth were greatly alarmed, thinking that the problem had become serious. After investigation, it was learned that there were more than 500 bandits on the border of Suiyuan at that time, and the Sui army was dispatched to suppress them. Since then, the number of bandits has gradually increased to two or three thousand, so the bandit suppression army has also been increased. The outside world's claim that there are two regiments or even two divisions of the Japanese army supervising the battle behind the bandits is ridiculous. Japan believes that China, whether it is Eastern Sui or other regions, is Chinese territory, and everything should be carried out in accordance with the principles of Sino-Japanese friendship and cooperation. The bandit disturbances in Eastern Sui have nothing to do with Japan."

According to foreign sources, since the establishment of the Hirota Cabinet in Japan, its general policy has not yet been fully determined. Some advocate a "southward advance policy," which is to seize rights and interests in the South Seas, but this raises many concerns with Britain and the United States. Others advocate a "northward advance policy," which is to patrol and occupy Inner Mongolia to resist Russia, with North China as the next priority. However, if Inner Mongolia is immediately seized, there are also considerations regarding the Soviet Union. Due to the environment and other factors, which steps to take are currently undecided. Therefore, the rumored changes in the situation in the outside world are not necessarily true at present. However, it is true that those who want to get promoted are stirring up trouble in the middle. The Eastern Sui issue was largely caused by this. Others were prepared, and there was nothing they could do. Ultimately, the situation in Inner Mongolia will be serious, which is also a planned scheme by others. (14th)

Lu Salt Export to Japan Is About to Be Realized; The First Batch Is 70,000 Tons; The Lu Feng Store Has Been Established 58

Tianjin Dispatch: The export of Lu salt to Japan has been repeatedly discussed between Japanese commissioners Kaneshiro Kawanishi and Vice Consul Junichi Nagai and the Changlu Salt Transport Office and the Export Office. The export methods and purchase procedures have been specifically agreed upon. However, regarding the tax rate, the Ministry of Finance originally stipulated a tax of one yuan per ton, but the Japanese side expressed disagreement and requested that the precedent of Qingdao salt export be followed, with a tax of 96 cents per ton. The Transport Office has telegraphed the Ministry of Finance for instructions, and it is expected that there will be no problem. The major matters can be realized in advance at the end of this month. According to Liu Renfu, the section chief of the Export Office, the Lu Feng Store, a Lu salt export merchant, has been approved by the Ministry of Finance and officially started business yesterday. The store is indeed composed of various beach households, so Shao Jingyin, the chairman of the Beach Industry Association, has been appointed as the manager to take full responsibility. The office is temporarily located in Hangu, and it is planned to establish a branch or office here in the future for close liaison. Next, the more than 50 tons of salt stored in Hangu will be exported as a priority to help the beach households there. We are now waiting for the Japanese side to purchase. According to Japanese Vice Consul Nagai, "The Lu salt export method has been completely agreed upon. Only the tax rate is slightly higher than that of Qingdao. After negotiations with the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee, it is no longer a problem. Currently, our country urgently needs industrial salt, so we will advance its realization within this month. The first batch is 70,000 tons. After it is transported to Japan, we will continue to purchase. Within days, we will instruct Mitsubishi, Iwai, Toyo Soda, and other importing merchants to contact the Lu Feng Store to purchase salt." (14th)

Chahar Construction Department Plans to Restore the Longyan Iron Mine; Sends Personnel for Inspection and Formulates Restoration Opinions; The Hebei-Chahar Construction Committee Submits to the Economic Committee for Review 59

Zhangjiakou Dispatch: Yantong Mountain, two li north of Xuanhua County, Chahar Province, is rich in red iron ore. Longguan County produces magnetic iron ore. The ore vein is sixty li long and has extremely rich reserves and quality that ranks first in the country. The former Longyan Iron Mining Company was a joint venture between the government and merchants with a capital of 5 million yuan in the seventh year of the Republic of China. It managed the mining and applied for a mining area of 42 square li and 375 mu. Initially, it was planned to smelt iron locally, but due to many inconveniences, the iron smelting plant was changed to Shijingshan in western Beiping. Equipment for mining and smelting was largely in place, but due to the exhaustion of capital and the inability to continue, it has been suspended to this day. Recently, the Chahar Provincial Construction Department sent Li Fengcen to inspect. After returning to the department, in addition to reporting the suspension situation, he also formulated opinions on increasing capital and restoring the mine. After the Chahar Construction Department reviewed it, Zhang Lisheng and Qiao Shibing of the Hebei-Chahar Construction Committee submitted it to the Construction Committee for resolution and transferred it to the Hebei-Chahar Economic Committee for review. The proposals of Zhang and Qiao are recorded as follows:

The original proposal reads, "Mining is one of the important productions. The coal mining in Chahar Province has made progress in recent years. More than 60 mining operations have been licensed for mining, but there is not a single metal mine that has been mined and smelted. Gold, silver, copper, and lead mines may be due to incomplete exploration and the treasures are buried, or due to the lack of drilling and mining, the reserves are unknown, and waiting to be managed. The Xuanhua Yantong Mountain and Longguan Iron Mine are uniquely rich in accumulation and rank first in the country, but have not yet resumed work, which is a pity. Recently, in order to understand the current situation of the iron mine in the area, the head of the Second Section of this department, Li Feng, was sent to inspect. After he returned, he reported the situation of the continued suspension and submitted opinions. The content of the report is 'Opinions on the restoration of the Longyan Iron Mine, requesting review and approval, and to be implemented in order to lay the foundation for the basic industry of North China.' The Longyan Iron Mining Company was the first to mine Pangjiabao and Xinyao in Longguan County, with a total area of 25 square li and 195 mu. A license was issued on June 21 of the seventh year of the Republic of China. The company was named Longguan. Then, on November 2 of the same year, the former Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce issued a mining license for Yantong Mountain in Xuanhua County, with an area of 17 square li and 180 mu. The three places total 42 square li and 375 mu and were renamed to the current name. The ore quality is all red iron ore, but Longguan also produces magnetic iron ore. The mineral quality of Longguan Iron Mine is purer than that of Xuanhua County. In summary, the iron content of the iron ore ranges from 45% to 65%, with an average of over 50%. The iron ore reserves are 100 million tons. During the Longguan Company period, there was a proposal to build a branch road from Xuanhua to Pangjiabao. After the addition of the Yantong Mountain mining area, it was closely connected to Xuanhua Station. A 16-hua li branch road was built by the former Beijing-Suiyuan Railway Bureau from the station around the western suburbs of the county to the Shuimo Station, about two li north of the city. A light railway of eight hua li was built from Shuimo to the north to the mining mountain. Shuimo Station was used as the starting point for transporting ore. At this time, Yantong Mountain was mined first, and Longguan was operated later. The construction of the Pangjiabao branch road was discussed from Sui. The original plan for the mining and treatment of Yantong Mountain Iron Ore was to smelt iron locally. A limestone plant was surveyed and determined at Baobao Mountain in Huailai County, and coal mines of 29 square li, 150 mu, and 4,758 square chi were measured and claimed in Baicaoyao, Huangyazi, and Wucha in Yu County. Six hundred mu of land were purchased in the west of Xuanhua City as a site for building factories and setting up furnaces. The solvent was taken from Huailai, and the fuel was supplied from Yu County. This was the original design. Later, the Shijingshan Station on the Pingmen Road was adjacent to the capital, and its location was superior. The Zhaizhai coal and coke could be purchased nearby, so there was no need to operate the coal industry. The coal and coke in the Sixhegou coal mine and the major mines in Hebei, which were suitable for iron smelting, could be transferred by train. The limestone in General's Mausoleum was pure in texture and was considered the best in metallurgy. The area was located on the Yongding River in the lower reaches of the Yang River, so there was no shortage of water. All of this was beyond the reach of Xuanhua, so the idea of iron smelting in Xuanhua was abandoned, and the decision to build a factory in Shijingshan was made. The major details were obtained, and all kinds of equipment, such as houses, furniture, and related mining and iron smelting, as well as transportation equipment, and all replacement parts, were largely prepared. In particular, a railway was built from the General's Mausoleum Limestone Plant to Sanjiadian Station on the Pingmen Road and two iron furnaces, one completed and one uncompleted, in Shijingshan consumed a lot of money. From the establishment of the company to the suspension, a total of 6 million national currency was spent, exceeding the original amount of 5 million yuan in shares by a significant amount. This is the general situation of the Longyan Company. After the company was suspended, the Ministry of Agriculture and Mines of the National Government established the Longyan Mining Bureau around the 17th year of the Republic of China and planned to resume work, but due to pending funding, the Ministry of Railways was assigned to take custody of it. In August of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, the Northwest Development Association came to Chahar and held its second annual meeting. The meeting proposed the restoration of the Xuanlong Iron Mine to extract this 100 million tons of treasure and requested the Ministry of Railways to allocate 3 million yuan for the restoration work to establish the most fundamental foundation for developing the Northwest with the fastest and most effective results. It has been shelved until now. Iron is to the country as food is to the farmer. If the farmer eats but does not cultivate, he will inevitably sell it, abandon it, and be invaded by others. The same is true of iron mines. Now, the mines along the Yangtze River, such as Daye Elephant Nose Mountain, are sold to the eastern neighbors to extract value, which is mining in reality. The mines in Benxihu and Anshan in southern Manchuria have long been in the hands of foreigners, which is being invaded. Longyan's decline is abandonment. If it is sold, abandoned, or invaded, the country's use of iron will remain the same. The customs trade register shows that the customs trade of steel imports averages between 400,000 and 600,000 tons per year, which can be counted as 500,000 tons. Of the steel imported from Jiangzhe and the Yangtze River customs, 200,000 tons account for 40% of the country, 150,000 tons imported from the Northeast customs account for 30% of the country, 50,000 tons imported from the Minyue Guidian customs account for 11%, and 100,000 tons imported from the Lu customs account for 20%. The country absorbs such a huge amount of foreign iron, and the Longyan Iron Mine's reserves are so large. It is a pity to allow it to be abandoned. The Ministry of Industry has tried to set up a steel plant. It first set up a plant in Pukou, then focused on Ma'anshan, and finally focused on Xiejiadian. The iron sand sought to obtain small mines in Anhui with reserves of 100,000, 200,000, and even millions of tons. Although it has not been completed, it has been actively discussed. The Longyan Iron Mine, which has a magnificent scale and failed to achieve success, was abandoned like a legacy, allowing foreign goods to arrive one after another, and the national treasures were sealed. If this continues, there will be those who surpass it. In order to avoid the situation and seek remedial measures, there is no way to go other than to choose one of the two methods: continued investment by government and people or joint investment between China and foreign countries. Continued investment by government and people should be gradually increased. The initial additional amount should be 5 million yuan. The government funds should still be the amount determined by the Northwest Development Association, with 3 million yuan allocated by the central government as government shares. The remaining 2 million yuan should be shared by the merchants and people of the counties under Hebei, Chahar, and Shandong and the cities of Beiping and Tianjin. It is reported that the Guangdong Provincial Government, due to the provincial iron plant also operating coal mines, applied to the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board for a huge loan, which has been approved by the Board at its 36th meeting in Beijing to borrow 4 million yuan for Sichuan to repair the Chengpeng Railway and mine copper and iron in Peng County by the Military Commission. The Hunan Liujia Coal Mine Industry Department borrowed 2 million yuan for development. The Shaanxi Provincial Government, seeing the progress of the development of the Northwest, urgently needs to drill and explore government coal fields and agreed with the Economic Committee to assist and the China Construction Bank to lend 3 million yuan. Although Xuanlong is a remote area, it is also a national domain and should not be discriminated against. If the Economic Committee and the two ministries of Iron and Steel or the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board are requested to allocate 3 million yuan, it should be easy. As for the people's support, the number of shares should be allocated to counties and cities as units, and stock certificates should be issued with numbers, with a minimum investment of ten yuan per share, allowing merchants and people to freely sell and buy, but not allowing them to leave the territory of the counties and cities. In the future, if the mining industry has surplus profits, the list will be checked and remitted, and the competent authorities of the provincial and municipal governments will distribute them in batches, and the merchants and people will be made aware that iron making is related to their livelihoods and is different from general investment for profit. In this way, the 2 million yuan in shares can be easily raised. This is the method of continued investment by government and people. Joint investment between China and foreign countries should be on a large scale. The total amount should first be 50 million yuan. In addition to the 6 million yuan of Chinese investment that has been used, foreign investment should first join the same amount of shares, and the remaining amount should be paid equally by both parties when expanding operations. Foreign investment does not distinguish between countries, nor between government and business. All friendly countries that are willing to invest are accepted. The company's affairs, unless otherwise specified, shall be handled in accordance with the Chinese Mining Law, Company Law, and other related laws. After the joint investment between China and foreign countries is agreed upon, in order to facilitate the collection of affairs, a Longyan Iron Mining Delegation must be established. The old government and merchant shareholders, the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee, and the provincial governments where the mining areas are located shall each send one person as a representative, and the representatives shall jointly elect one person as the chief representative to preside over the solicitation of foreign investment. The delegation address should also be set up in Beiping for convenience. This is another method of joint investment between China and foreign countries. The above two methods are proposed to be submitted by this department to the Provincial Government Committee for review and approval and then transferred to the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee for adoption, reference, and implementation in order to establish the basic industry of North China. Whether the proposal is appropriate, please review."

It is said that the various sections mentioned by the section chief are not without merit. If the Longyan Iron Mine is restored, not only will the industry of Chahar Province be revitalized, but also the neighboring provinces will benefit from it. The statement of establishing the basic industry of North China is probably not an exaggeration. However, how to proceed in the end, in addition to already sending a letter to the Hebei-Chahar Economic Committee for review, it is reasonable to record the case and submit it for public decision.

New News on Smuggling Case

The patrol team of the Public Security Bureau previously arrested Zhang Wang, a woman who was smuggling artificial silk at the station, along with more than 30 catties of artificial silk and three bills of lading from Hengtong Transport Company. Together with officials from the Suzhou Customs, they seized two packages of artificial silk, totaling 39 catties, inside the Hengtong Transport Company, which is being verified. A large number of paper goods seized by the General Labor Union were not within the designated scope of smuggling and have been released separately.

Police Officer Commits Suicide by Poisoning

Sun Zhifan, a police officer from the Fourth Sub-Station directly under the Urban District of the Public Security Bureau, is 32 years old. He committed suicide by poisoning because he was madly in love with a prostitute, Zhong Xiuying, and squandered public funds. He was taken to the County Hospital for rescue but died on the morning of the 16th. Sun Zhifan is a native of another province and has served in the police force for many years. He is capable and valued by the inspection officers of the station. The station's rent donations were all handled by Police Officer Sun. He made monthly settlements but was recently bewitched by a Suzhou prostitute, Zhong Xiuying, and his love was very hot, so he used up the rent donations he had collected. He initially planned to find a way to make up for it, but the new director is about to take over in Changshu, and all the taxes and donations collected should be handed over, so Police Officer Sun could not transfer the funds. On the night of the 14th of this month, he secretly swallowed sleeping pills and committed suicide. He was discovered the next morning and immediately sent to the County Hospital, but he died this morning due to severe poisoning. He left behind many letters, all stating his love for the prostitute and his deep regret for his past mistakes, and asking Inspection Officer Yan Shaoye to advance the arrears and he would repay him in the next life.

Ningbo 66

Tax Police Shoot Innocent Civilians

Tangtou Street in Hanling Market, east of Yin County, is a vital route to Xianxiang and Dasong. Every 2nd, 4th, and 8th day of the month is market day, and residents from dozens of miles around come to buy and sell goods. On the 14th, which was a market day, Zhou Xiangsheng from Tongxia Mountain and Ye Yuesheng from Dasha Mountain carried mountain goods to the market. After selling their goods, they used the proceeds to buy rice and head home. When they passed Dongqing Bridge in Xianxiang, several tax police officers from Dasong, dressed in plain clothes, were patrolling. Seeing the two men hurrying along with heavy loads, they suspected them of carrying smuggled salt and ordered them to stop. Zhou and Ye, because it was almost noon and their families were waiting for rice for lunch, coupled with the scorching sun and the distance still to home, and because they did not understand the local dialect, were unaware that these men were investigating smuggled salt. Therefore, they continued hurrying as before. This further aroused the suspicion of the tax police, who fired two shots at their lower bodies. The two men fell to the ground after being hit. The tax police went forward to inspect and, upon seeing that it was rice, realized their mistake. They left without regard for the injured men's lives. Later, some villagers passing by notified the families of the two men, who carried them to the Yin County Local Court for examination of their injuries and then sent them to the Chinese-American Hospital in the city for treatment.
