Your newspaper's report is entirely inconsistent with the facts, and I fear it will confuse the public. In addition to pursuing legal action, I am writing to request that your newspaper issue a correction. Respectfully, Shen Wenzhi, Town Head of Shi Qiao Town.

Report on the Achievements of the Rockefeller Foundation in China 68

— Gu Huimin

The Rockefeller Foundation of the United States has a long history of supporting educational endeavors in China, especially in medicine and natural sciences. In 1935, the foundation began to show a tendency to assist rural reconstruction efforts. In 1935, the foundation's funds for the "China Program" could be divided into five major categories, as listed below:

1935 Foundation Appropriations in China

(1) North China Program

Chinese Mass Education Promotion Association: National currency 50,000 yuan

Nankai University Institute of Economics: 37,500 yuan

Yenching University School of Social Sciences and School of Science: 77,325 yuan

(2) Nanjing Public Health and Medical Program

National Health Administration: National currency 87,500 yuan

Medical Education Committee: 21,250 yuan

(3) Jinling Agricultural Program

Jinling University Department of Agricultural Economics: US$5,500

Department of Natural Sciences: National currency 72,500 yuan

National Central University College of Agriculture (Animal Husbandry and Veterinary Medicine): 34,600 yuan

Agricultural Experiment Station (Control work): 34,300 yuan

(4) Scholarships US$37,500

Subsidies

Subsidies for research and development US$10,000

North China Program

The higher education institutions in North China that receive subsidies from the Foundation include Nankai University in Tianjin and Yenching University in Peiping. The Dingxian Mass Education Promotion Association also receives its support.

The Dingxian Mass Education Promotion Association received an appropriation of National currency 150,000 yuan from the Foundation. This association is dedicated to rural reconstruction, originally established for the mass literacy movement, and has now become a well-organized institution for educational practice and research. This planned mass education movement is beyond the financial capacity of the local area, and therefore urgently needs external funding. Training in self-government, public security, education, people's livelihood, and public health is conducted under simple and economical principles. The association is currently engaged in the training of village government personnel, in order to expand this pilot program to the whole country. As for the original intention of the Foundation, it is to assist university graduates in engaging in rural training and to study new methods of rural reconstruction.

This cooperative program began on July 1st of last year. The Dingxian Mass Education Association now has a Special Training Committee, which has established 37 domestic scholarships in the fields of education, health, local administration, agriculture, and economics. In fact, Dingxian has become a training experiment center, with the pilot area being extended to Guangxi, Hunan, Guangdong, Sichuan, Henan, and other provinces.

The Nankai University Institute of Economics received an appropriation of National currency 37,500 yuan from the Foundation. The purpose of the appropriation is to support the institute's teaching and research on rural reconstruction issues and to enable the institute to maintain close contact with the Dingxian Mass Education Area. Several graduates of the Nankai University Institute of Economics have gone to Dingxian for further training. The institute has added courses such as Cooperative Studies, Land Administration, Local Administration, and Local Finance. Several students have been assigned to various counties for eight months of practical training to prepare them for rural administrative positions. Seven domestic scholarships have also been established in the new courses.

Yenching University School of Social Sciences and School of Science received an appropriation of National currency 58,125 yuan from the Foundation, and the School of Social Sciences received an additional National currency 9,200 yuan for the development of rural reconstruction training courses. In addition to continuing to run pre-medical and pre-nursing courses, Yenching University has also established a new social science program, the purpose of which is to train young people to take on social and economic work such as local administration, rural administration, rural education, and peasant side occupations. Yenching University has also formed a committee with Nankai University and the Dingxian Mass Education Association to carry out planned programs. Since last year, Yenching University has established new rural courses, all of which are taught by full-time faculty.

The Yenching University School of Science has received assistance from the Rockefeller Foundation in recent years and is now also turning its attention to rural issues. The Department of Biology focuses on the study of entomology, and the Department of Chemistry is exploring rural side occupations such as pottery and leather making.

The three departments of the Yenching University School of Social Sciences have added as many as eleven new rural problem courses. 119 students have enrolled. In addition, there are special research classes in Cooperative Studies and Local Administration. For experimental purposes, the school's professor of sociology has been appointed as the county head of a county with a population of 300,000. Graduates in economics and political science are interning in the county. The general interest in rural issues is evident from this.

Nanjing Public Health and Medical Program

Under this program, the National Health Administration and the Medical Education Committee receive subsidies from the Foundation. This public health training is very important for China's reconstruction.

The National Health Administration received an appropriation of National currency 87,500 yuan from the Foundation, mostly for the training of medical and health personnel. The National Health Administration has added staff, purchased equipment, and enriched various courses in teaching, including several specifically designed for nurses, medical officers, and health inspectors. There are 51 scholarships, the purpose of which is to train health medical officers, nurses, sanitation engineers, and rural health workers. (To be continued)

Local News

City Chamber of Commerce and Other Groups Held Civic Oath Ceremony Yesterday Morning / Chairman Du Yuesheng Led the Entire Swearing-In / City Farmers' Association and Others Held Ceremonies Separately 69

According to Xin Sheng She, the members and staff of the City Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations held a civic oath ceremony at 9:00 AM yesterday in the City Chamber of Commerce auditorium. Over 1,000 people attended, including Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Gu Xinyi, Xu Jiqing, Jin Runxiang, Ke Ganchen, Ge Jiecun, and Hu Xiyuan. Chairman Du Yuesheng led the entire body in taking the oath and then delivered a speech, saying, "Everyone, today we are holding a civic oath ceremony here. As for the significance of civic registration, it is purely for the election of the National Assembly. After we swear and register, we will obtain the right to elect and be elected. At the same time, we should pay more attention to following the oath, renewing the old and welcoming the new, upholding the Republic of China, and striving for regeneration, so as to promote the prosperity of the country and the nation."

Supervisor Wang Manyun's Admonition

Next, supervisor Wang Manyun gave an admonitory speech, saying, "We are here today to swear an oath, swearing that from today onwards, we will renew the old and welcome the new, and pledge our loyalty to uphold the Republic of China, follow the teachings of the Premier, and implement the Three Principles of the People. After taking the oath today, we are citizens of the Republic of China. We are cells in the entire organization of the Republic of China, and our relationship with the Republic of China is united as one. If the Republic of China is a steel machine, then we are the screws in this machine. If the Republic of China is a cement building, then we are every cement stone that makes up this cement building. For thousands of years, the Republic of China has suffered from innate weaknesses in its internal feudal politics and acquired damages from 20th-century imperialism. We should now take on the responsibility of protecting the Republic of China and building a new life for the Republic of China. We should always practice our oath and step onto the great era of struggle and regeneration in order to seek a bright future for the Chinese nation. Only then will we not fail our oath today, and only then will we not fail our responsibility as citizens."

Cocoon Merchants Scheduled to Meet to Discuss Autumn Cocoon Purchasing Methods 71

According to Xin Sheng She, the Jiangzhe autumn silkworm rearing season has begun. The Cocoon Industry Association has scheduled a joint meeting for the 23rd to discuss cocoon purchasing methods. Banks are handling loans for purchasing autumn cocoons. Details are as follows:

Seed Distribution in Two Provinces

After the Zhejiang Provincial Sericulture Control Committee's control of silk cocoons proved effective, it was decided to continue the control method for this year's autumn cocoons, following the spring cocoon method. The autumn silkworm eggs have already been distributed to the county governments for distribution to the farmers who raise silkworms and are about to hatch. The Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Improvement Committee has also distributed this year's autumn silkworm seeds to the county governments, allowing them to be distributed to farmers starting today. Silk factories and leftover cocoon merchants who wish to purchase this year's autumn cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces must register with the silk cocoon authorities of the two provinces.

Cocoon Merchant Meeting

The Zhejiang Provincial Cocoon Industry Association has decided to hold a meeting in Hangzhou at 2:00 PM on the 23rd of this month because the autumn silkworms have begun to hatch, to discuss this year's autumn cocoon purchasing methods. Mr. Chu Huiseng, Chairman of the Association, made a special report at the joint meeting of the Shanghai, Zhejiang, and Wuxi Silk Factory Industry Associations yesterday, inviting all silk factory colleagues who wish to purchase this year's autumn cocoons in Zhejiang Province to attend the meeting on the 23rd to discuss the process together. Shanghai silk factories have also prepared to organize an autumn cocoon purchasing agency to handle cocoon purchasing matters.

Bank Loans

The 22 banks and money houses including the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Shanghai Bank had excellent results from organizing the Jiangzhe Cocoon Purchasing Loan Syndicate in the spring of 1936. Although it has now ended, because the output of autumn cocoons this year is less than that of spring cocoons, it was decided not to organize a syndicate again, but to have each bank handle it independently. The method will be the same as the previous syndicate method. Silk factories and leftover cocoon merchants who wish to purchase autumn cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces can contact the banks themselves to borrow money.

Silk Factories from Zhejiang, Wuxi, and Shanghai Held a Joint Meeting Yesterday to Discuss Improving Raw Silk Inspection Procedures 72

According to Da Gong She, the Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Association convened a joint meeting of silk factories from Zhejiang, Wuxi, and Shanghai at 4:00 PM yesterday at the Suzhou-Zhejiang-Anhui Silk Cocoon General Office on North Shanxi Road to discuss improving raw silk quality inspection procedures. Several important methods were decided. Details are as follows:

Attending Representatives

The attendees included Shen Huachen, Chen Zezhong, Zhang Yunsheng, Tang Yeqin (representing Cao Jinsheng), Huang Jiwen, and Zhang Peishen from Shanghai; Chu Huiseng and Ye Jingshi from Zhejiang; and Cheng Bingruo, Zheng Haiquan, Wang Huanan, Zhang Jifang, and Cao Shaochen from Wuxi. Shen Huachen was elected chairman.

Chairman's Report

After the formalities were completed, Chairman Shen Huachen first reported on the two purposes of the meeting: (1) Since the Commodity Inspection Bureau implemented raw silk quality inspection on the 1st of this month, the inspection methods have created obstacles for both buyers and sellers of raw silk. First, the receipt form issued by the bureau for silk submitted for inspection is improper. Second, the public weighing fee for inspecting quality is set at 25 yuan per bale, which is excessive waste. Third, the inspection was originally scheduled to be completed in two days, but in reality, it is delayed to four days. (2) The Raw Silk Exporters Association held a meeting on the 5th of this month and resolved on five methods, the most important of which is the 25-strand raw silk sample strip issue. Our silk factory colleagues cannot tacitly agree to this. In summary, we should jointly discuss response methods.

Methods Decided

After the report, discussions began immediately. Representatives from the silk factories in Zhejiang, Wuxi, and Shanghai expressed their opinions one after another. The following resolutions were passed: A. Five methods for requesting the Commodity Inspection Bureau to improve its raw silk quality inspection procedures: (1) Request the Commodity Inspection Bureau to improve the receipt form to show caution. (2) Request to increase inspection efficiency (with the principle that inspection should be completed within two days) to benefit silk merchants. (3) Regarding the issue of public weighing fee waste, request the bureau to simplify the application procedures, allowing silk merchants to report and verify the quality first and then pay the public weighing fee if necessary, in order to avoid sacrifices. (4) Request the bureau to allow silk merchants to have the right to request a free re-inspection once. (5) Request the bureau not to limit the inspection certificate to five bales as a batch, but allow ten bales to be classified as a batch to avoid the drawback that each batch does not meet the 78 cm standard and is not allowed to be declared for export. B. Countermeasures against the five resolutions of the Exporters Association on August 5th: (1) We decide that the Exporters Association's resolution that after August 5th, the 25 silk strands (i.e., sample strips) inspected by silk factories selling silk to export firms should belong to the exporter. (2) When exporters conduct their own inspection, one sample is drawn from each bale. Now that the government agency has been changed to conduct the inspection, exporters should no longer need to draw samples for inspection. (3) The goods should be delivered directly by the manufacturer to the Commodity Inspection Bureau, believing that there is no need to deliver them to the exporter first. (4) Request the Commodity Inspection Bureau to postpone the announcement of the raw silk grade inspection standards and the implementation date of the inspection. (According to the grade inspection layer, the Commodity Inspection Bureau has scheduled to implement it on February 1st of next year. On the 5th of this month, the Exporters Association convened a general meeting to resolve to urge the government to implement this grade inspection as soon as possible, but the silk factory industry opposes the Exporters Association's claim). (5) Delivery of futures should be submitted to the Commodity Inspection Bureau for inspection no later than the 26th of each month. If there is a holiday, it may be extended. (6) The method of collecting money for raw silk transactions should be cancelled, and the exporter should immediately pay the full amount of the goods upon completion of inspection based on the public weighing slip, in accordance with the principle of cash on delivery. This will be implemented from September 1st. Before the exporters express their agreement, the delivery of September futures will be temporarily suspended. The above methods will be recorded and notified to the Exporters Association for reference. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Scheduled Consultation

After the meeting, Shen Huachen told the Da Gong She reporter that regarding the implementation of raw silk quality inspection, the exporter side (i.e., the buyer) and the silk merchant (i.e., the seller) have different opinions due to different positions. The Exporters Association convened a general meeting on the 5th of this month to resolve five methods regarding all transaction issues after the implementation of raw silk inspection. Silk merchants naturally find it difficult to agree because there are conflicts of interest with their own interests. In order to take into account the interests of both buyers and sellers in raw silk transactions, it has been decided that each of the silk factories in Zhejiang, Wuxi, and Shanghai will each send two representatives to consult with the Exporters Association at a later date. Director Miao Zhongxiu of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau will also be invited to attend and provide instructions so that a satisfactory solution can be obtained.

Amidst the Arrival of New Rice / Agricultural Warehouses Are Built One After Another / Spreading Throughout the Provinces of the Country and Deep into the Countryside / Meeting the Urgent Needs of Extraordinary Times 74

According to Hua Dong She, this year's new rice and early rice have already been harvested, and late rice will also be available in a month. Agricultural warehouses in various provinces have been established one after another. Details are as follows:

Agricultural Warehouse Completion

Under the supervision of the Ministry of Industry and the guidance of the former National Economic Commission's Cooperative Affairs Committee, and with the voluntary efforts of the people in various provinces and cities, agricultural association warehouses have been completed after about three years, in line with the needs of the times. In total, each province of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangxi has one warehouse per county. Some of these warehouses are built by the province, some by the county, and some are operated automatically by the people with the support of economists and financiers. To date, they are sufficient for use.

Deep into the Countryside

These warehouses are the latest type of construction. Although there is no need for great buildings in the countryside, they are more ventilated and suitable for lighting than the rice barns built by farmers themselves. New and old grains can be stored for three or four years without spoiling, so they are highly trusted by farmers. However, in some villages, there are many local bullies who manipulate this new organization, just like bacteria mixed into cells, and farmers are very wary of them.

Concurrent Pawn Shop Operations

These warehouses are very suitable for emergency needs in extraordinary times. However, researchers of rural economics believe that warehouses have the opportunity to be utilized during the preparation period, and it is necessary to concurrently operate pawn shops. Farmers can temporarily pawn their farm implements and small valuables for use when they need them, and redeem them at a low interest rate during busy farming seasons, and use this as a revolving fund for small-scale side-farming economies.

Banks Handle Loans for the Transportation and Sale of Rice and Wheat / The Government Passes Relief Measures for Transportation and Sale / Japanese Merchants' Purchase of Wheat Drives Prices Up 75

According to Xin Sheng She, this year's wheat crop has been a bumper harvest in all wheat-producing areas of the country. According to the calculations of the Nanjing Rice and Wheat Improvement Institute, the wheat production is 495 million jins. In particular, the wheat produced in the provinces of Shandong and Hebei in North China is of the best quality, and the wheat grains are larger than foreign wheat. This year's early rice has been a bumper harvest in rice-producing areas, and early and late rice will also be harvested one after another. Due to the favorable weather, it is predicted that there will also be a bumper harvest. The Executive Yuan has approved seven relief measures for the transportation and sale of rice and wheat in response to the request of the Hubei Provincial Government, and has ordered them to be followed.

Bank Loans

All banks that operate savings businesses have decided to handle various agricultural loans with at least one-fifth of the total savings amount, in accordance with Articles 7 and 8 of the Savings Bank Law. The total savings deposits in various banks is 600 million yuan. If one-fifth is calculated, it would be 120 million yuan. Banks handle agricultural loans, with rice, wheat, and cotton being the main agricultural products. The loan methods are divided into production and transportation and sale. The production period of rice, wheat, and cotton is about to pass, so banks such as the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Bank, the China Farmers Bank, and the Jin Cheng Bank have already started handling loans for the transportation and sale of rice and wheat.

Japanese Merchants' Purchase

Since the Japanese Mitsui and Mitsubishi companies purchased wheat in our country's wheat-producing areas and loaded it onto ships to Japan for flour mills to produce flour, they are still continuing to purchase. As of yesterday, more than 300,000 dans had been loaded and exported. The price of wheat has risen due to the purchase by Japanese merchants. The current price of wheat is 5 yuan per 100-jin bag. The Chinese government is consulting with the Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance on specific measures for the wheat export issue. As for the rumors that Japanese merchants are buying our country's rice, it is still difficult to verify.

Business, Agricultural, and Social Organizations Held a Public Memorial Service for Wu Xingya Yesterday, Presided Over by Wang Xiaolai, Yu Zhenyun, and Others 80

After the coffin of the late Wu Xingya, member of the Central Committee and Standing Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, was transported to Shanghai, various sectors of the city have been holding public memorial services for several days in memory of him. Yesterday was the last day of the public memorial service. In the morning, the business community held a public memorial service, and in the afternoon, social organizations and the agricultural community held a public memorial service. The coffin is temporarily placed in the China Funeral Parlor. After Mayor Wu lights the spirit tablet on an auspicious day, he will be buried. The funeral preparation committee has also decided to hold a memorial meeting, which is currently being prepared. The details are recorded as follows:

Business Organizations

At 10:00 AM yesterday, more than 100 trade associations, including the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the banking industry, the jewelry industry, the miscellaneous grain industry, the shipping industry, the yarn industry, the sugar industry, the yarn factory industry, the porcelain industry, the cigarette industry, the rice shop industry, the cured meat industry, the chemical raw materials industry, the customs brokerage industry, and the tea processing industry, held a public memorial service. More than 100 people attended, including Qian Xinzhi, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Gu Yiyi, Xu Jilu, Hu Xiyuan, Shen Huachen, and Zheng Zenan. Wang Xiaolai presided over the memorial service, and Yan E-sheng read the memorial text. The memorial text is recorded as follows: "On the sixteenth day of August in the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and various trade associations respectfully offer clear wine and delicacies to the spirit of the late Director Wu Xingya of the Social Affairs Bureau, saying: 'Shanghai is a gateway to all nations. The establishment of a city and government requires the proper establishment of regulations. You, sir, with your great reputation, came to preside over industry and commerce, firmly upholding the overall situation, and taking measures with peace and order. You followed the rules and regulations, comparable to a hall. You spent half your life on horseback, secretly harming your body and spirit. You have been bedridden for years, like Ji An in Huaiyang. Mount Lu is bright and beautiful, a scenic spot for immortals. You moved to nourish your illness, choosing a better place. We hoped for your recovery, comforting this side. But alas, you sang the funeral song, and your coffin was returned. The city shed tears, all over the棠疆 (Tang Jiang). We offer sacrifices in your position, and respectfully present this cup. May your spirit come and enjoy this offering. Respectfully, we offer this sacrifice.'"

Agricultural and Social Organizations

From 2:00 PM in the afternoon, social organizations held a public memorial service. More than a hundred representatives from dozens of social organizations, including the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, the China Animal Protection Association, the Shanghai Branch of the Red Cross Society, the Cooperative Enterprise Committee, the Jiangning Six Counties Fellow-Provincials Association, and the Jushenghe Sports Association, attended. Liu Wanqing and Zai Yan presided over the memorial service. At 4:00 PM in the afternoon, the Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association and the farmers' associations of various districts held a public memorial service. Shan Yu Zhen presided over the memorial service. The memorial text is recorded below: "On the sixteenth day of August in the twenty-fifth year of the Republic of China, the entire staff of the Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association and the farmers' associations of various districts respectfully offer clear wine and flowers to the spirit of Mr. Wu Xingya, saying: 'Alas, our sir, the hero of the three Chu states, with the spirit of Hubei and Yue, and with the strategy of a military strategist. In times of chaos, you carried your strategy far and righteously, boarding a chariot and surveying the territory, and投明 (Tou Ming) for thousands of miles. You followed the army to the Lingbiao region, and sent messages to Beijing. You swept across the land, and the world became clear. You served as a public servant, and repeatedly received special honors. You 分藩滬凟 (Fen Fan Hu Du), and opened a government in Wancheng. Your virtuous administration remains on the stele, and your path is followed. How could we have expected the 二豎 (Er Shu) to be so deeply ingrained, nourishing your illness in Mount Lu, and suddenly 言薨 (Yan Hong)? The news spread, and the city and fields were shocked. Work stopped, and farming ceased. All our comrades could not help but cry out. We call your soul on the sea, looking up to your sincere spirit. We pour out our wine and offer our condolences, hoping you will accept our sincerity. Alas, alas, may you enjoy our sacrifice.'" The memorial texts of the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, the Jiangning Six Counties Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, and the Jushenghe Sports Association are omitted.

Shanghai Local Court Streamlines Entry Management 82

Since the newly appointed President Lu Yimei took office in the Shanghai Local Court, it has been found that there are often idlers mixed in the court. In order to streamline the gate posts and prohibit idlers from entering, starting from today, lawyers who come to the court to appear in court must enter the court building by presenting their lawyer badges. Even lawyers' clerks and other people who come to the court for business should also obtain entry and exit permits before they are allowed to enter. The parties concerned can enter the court with summonses or notices. The Lawyers Association was notified yesterday to check and implement this.

Domestic Wireless Telephone to be Completed as Ordered by the Ministry of Communications 84

According to the Dagon Press, the Ministry of Communications has decided to officially open the nine-province long-distance telephone network for communication on September 15. The Nanjing-Hankou-Peixian radio station is also being built actively. Domestic and foreign wireless telephones are required to be connected with various countries by the spring of next year. The following is a report from the Dagon Press reporter:

Nine-Province Telephone: The long-distance telephone network of the Ministry of Communications, covering nine provinces and cities including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hunan, Hubei, Sichuan, Shandong, Henan, Hebei, and Shanghai, has been completed for the five major trunk lines of Nanjing-Shanghai, Nanjing-Hankou, Nanjing-Tianjin, Jinan-Qingdao, and Beiping-Hankou. Several trial calls have been made in stages, with good results. Branch lines are currently being built. According to sources from the Shanghai transportation authorities, the nine-province long-distance telephone network is scheduled to be fully opened for communication on September 15. At that time, Minister Yu will preside over the communication ceremony in Nanjing and report on the construction process.

Nanjing-Hankou Radio Station: The audio amplification radio station for improving long-distance telephone equipment is located in Shanghai, Nanjing, and Hankou. Except for the Shanghai amplification station, which has been completed, the radio stations in Nanjing and Hankou have also been completed one after another. The audio amplifier is still being configured, and it is expected to be completed by the beginning of next month. Then, it will be used to exchange tests with the Shanghai amplification station.

Completion Required: Regarding the Shanghai, Hankou, and Guangzhou domestic wireless telephones, trial calls have been opened in Shanghai and Hankou. The official communication period and communication fees are being stipulated by the Ministry of Communications. As for Guangdong, since the Ministry of Communications sent personnel to organize it, the construction of the wireless telephone project has been actively accelerated. In addition, the international wireless telephones in various countries such as the United Kingdom, Germany, and the Philippines have been ordered by the International Radio Station to handle communications by February next year. New two-way telephones and telegraphs will continue to be purchased.

Lifting of Sanctions Against Italy: Improvement in Sino-Italian Trade 85

First batch transported over one hundred tons

According to the Shen Shi Press, since our country announced the lifting of sanctions against Italy on July 15, following the resolution of the League of Nations Executive Yuan, Sino-Italian trade has gradually returned to normal in the past half month. Italian goods exported to China, in addition to heavy industrial machinery, etc., are mainly artificial silk and olive oil. Our country's exports to Italy are mainly sesame, ramie, lime, and tung oil. Recently, the Italian ship "Victoria" exported sesame and other miscellaneous goods, reaching more than one hundred tons, which is a proof of the improvement of Sino-Italian trade relations after the lifting of sanctions against Italy.

Smoker Reporting Deadline 86

Municipal Anti-Opium Committee Assists with Guidance

According to the Dagon Press, the deadline for the general reporting of smokers in Shanghai was originally scheduled for August 10. In order to give the unregistered smokers a final chance to start anew, the Anti-Opium Supervisory Department of the Military Affairs Commission has approved an extension of the deadline until the end of this month. Therefore, the Municipal Public Security Bureau has been stepping up its investigation work in recent days. In order to assist the government in eliminating the atmosphere of opium, the Municipal Anti-Opium Committee has dispatched staff to various districts to carry out guidance, hoping that smokers will register as soon as possible or apply for admission to the hospital for treatment, so as to avoid criminal penalties. According to the report of the Smoker Registration Section of the Fourth Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, more than 200 smokers apply for registration every day last week.

Ziti Municipal Coordination Association Established 88

Ziti Town in West Shanghai (Zhudi) is under the jurisdiction of the Pusong District of Shanghai. Since the abolition of the Pusong Municipal Committee Office, although all municipal affairs have been directly handled by various municipal bureaus, it is inevitable that they cannot be reached due to the distance from Shanghai, resulting in the stagnation of construction in recent years. In view of this, the gentry of the town, Hou Shuda and Huang Chengbo, initiated the organization of the Ziti Municipal Coordination Association. Their call was met with enthusiastic responses and won the support of all sectors. After two months of preparation, it was officially established yesterday. Dozens of representatives from all sectors attended, and Hou Shuda, Hou Jilan, Huang Chengbo, Zhu Jinshu, Zhu Qinyuan, Ling Youjun, Tang Botao, Huang Shunbin, and Huang Shichang were elected as executive committee members on the spot. Hou Cheng, Zhang Danquan, Zhang Chunlin, Zai Jiefu, and Shen Meisun were elected as supervisory committee members. Hou Shuda, Hou Jilan, and Huang Chengbo were elected as standing committee members of the executive committee. Ling Youjun also served as the director of the secretariat, Zhu Qinyuan also served as the director of general affairs, Zhu Jinshu also served as the director of design, Tang Botao also served as the director of publicity, and Qian Kunfu served as the general manager. Three important cases were resolved on the spot: (A) Reporting to the party and government organs for record; (B) Submitting to the municipal authorities; (1) Requesting the repair of Pucao Zhai Road, (2) Dredging the Panlong River, which has been neglected for a long time, and (3) Constructing a prosperous bridge across the center; (C) Organizing a fundraising team, with Hou Junren as the commander, to raise funds to ensure its permanence. It was also recommended that Hou Shuda and Huang Chengbo draft the declaration, and work will begin immediately. From then on, the municipal construction of Zhudi will have a thriving image.

Accountant Shen Liren Discusses 90

The New News Agency reports: Yesterday, accountant Shen Liren presented his opinions on accounting issues following the implementation of income tax in our country. He offered many suggestions, which are recorded below.

Accounting Relationship

Our country's income tax will be levied starting next month. According to the provisional regulations on income tax promulgated by the national government, the taxation of for-profit businesses such as companies and firms is based on the ratio of capital to net profit. The determination of net profit is based on the income statement, and the figures in the income statement come from all account books. If the records in the account books do not match the facts, the calculation of net profit will inevitably be inaccurate, and the principle of fairness in taxation will be lost. Therefore, the quality of the accounting system of various businesses is closely related to the collection of income tax, which is obviously a logical conclusion. In the income tax laws and regulations of European and American countries, there are generally no restrictions on the accounting systems of various industries. This is because, although the accounting systems are not perfect, due to the widespread knowledge of accounting and the large number of accounting talents, the greatest force comes from schools and textbooks, so they have mostly become systematic. Each business has a unified accounting system that can be adopted. In contrast, in our country, except for banks, railways, and the government, which have unified accounting systems, other industrial and commercial enterprises, except for a small number, are chaotic and without any systematic organization. At the beginning of income tax collection, those in charge of various for-profit businesses will inevitably have two types of hesitations. One type is that although their business has a set accounting system, they are unsure whether it will pass inspection when they submit tax returns, and whether disputes will arise. They are also unsure whether their account books fully comply with the facts. The other type mainly consists of sole proprietorships or freelancers, where all income and expenses are managed by the owner personally. There is no need for an accounting system in the first place. Now, due to the collection of income tax, they must have detailed account books as the basis for filling out income tax returns, and they will inevitably have to establish an accounting system. However, how to establish it, and what the costs will be after its establishment, so that they do not suddenly increase, are all questions that cannot be easily resolved.

Innovating the System

It has been observed that the development of accounting in other countries has been promoted in part by the collection of income tax. Therefore, when our country implements this new tax, it is imperative to make a systematic reform of the accounting system for industry and commerce. The benefit is that it can promote the national industry in a big way, and reduce the occurrence of disputes during income tax collection in a small way. Therefore, I believe that the direct tax collection agency should hire those with rich experience and knowledge in accounting to organize an accounting system research association, divided into three groups: one for researching accounting subjects, one for researching account book formats, and another for researching fraud prevention methods. The current accounting subjects in our country, except for those stipulated by banks, railways, and government agencies, are mostly selected and created by various businesses themselves. It is often difficult for others to understand their meaning. Ordinary old-fashioned stores traditionally use auspicious phrases as the names of their account books, such as "taking righteousness as profit" to replace the final accounts report, and "bumper harvest" to replace sales, etc. As for new-style accountants, because what they have learned is all from English textbooks (mostly produced in the United States), the names of the subjects are mostly directly translated from English, such as "Accounts Receivable" translated as "應收賬項" (Yīngshōu zhàng xiàng, receivables), and "Surplus" translated as "盈餘" (Yíngyú, surplus). However, upon actual examination, subjects such as "Accounts Receivable" and "Surplus" were originally not very appropriate in English itself. They are only used because they have become customary. Our country does not research them and translates and uses them arbitrarily, which is even more erroneous. The research association should select the commonly used accounting subjects in our country, unify their names, and avoid discrepancies.

Unifying Account Books

The formats of various account books should vary depending on the nature of the business. However, ordinary basic account books, such as the journal, general ledger, and cash book, have the possibility of being unified. The research association should design the formats of these account books for the main industries for reference. As for books such as purchase and sales books, which must be changed according to the characteristics of the facts, they can be designed by hired accountants. In our country today, old-fashioned stores mostly continue to use the original Chinese account book formats. Newer stores either adopt the improved Chinese bookkeeping system of the transitional period or directly use the Western system. The so-called Western system is usually the British and American system, because those currently engaged in accounting work read English textbooks or English translations. Posting from various original books is done separately. However, what is actually used is also based on the continental system, emphasizing the journalized detailed book. The establishment of our country's accounting system originated in banks, and at that time, the Japanese banking system was used as a blueprint. The Japanese used the continental system. For this reason, modern accounting courses are often different from what is actually used. If the accounting system research association can be established and can formulate accounting systems for various industries, then various accounting textbooks must be rewritten to comply with laws and regulations. The fraud prevention methods research group specializes in researching internal controls for various transactions. Most industrial and commercial enterprises in our country employ many people, but due to the lack of a good internal control organization, fraud and errors cannot be prevented. If a slight change is made to comply with the principles of control, no expenses will be increased, and good results can be achieved.

Remedial Measures

The above is a description of the research work to be done on the accounting system in the future. However, since income tax will be levied soon, it is urgently necessary to determine a remedial method for businesses that do not yet have a good accounting system. Now, I will briefly present my views as follows. The businesses that urgently need remediation can still be divided into two categories, as mentioned earlier: one is those that already have an accounting system but it is not very suitable, and the other is those that have no accounting system at all. The former mainly consists of industrial and commercial enterprises, while the latter mostly consists of freelancers. First, let us discuss those with an existing accounting system. There are two preconditions for its improvement: first, not to increase expenses; and second, not to change the original staff. The method of improvement can still be carried out according to the principles of design. Now, I will describe them as follows: (1) Subject names: The government has previously promulgated a translated name for accounting subjects in our country, but it was only a small part. It can be used as a basis, and the same subjects that have been stipulated in the accounting of banks, railways, and the government can be used. The time for the change should be at the end of the month. (2) Fraud prevention methods: Depending on the number of employees used by the business, and within the possible scope, assign duties to the original staff and stipulate their responsibilities. Ensure that each transaction must be handled by at least two people so that they can check and balance each other. (3) Account book format: The account book format can be temporarily unchanged. However, it is necessary to investigate whether there is evidence of transaction records, from various documents to the account books, from the various account books to the general ledger, whether there are errors in the procedures, whether a third party can audit, and whether it is convenient to prepare reports from the general ledger. Those that do not meet these points should be reformed. As for businesses that have no account books, they should keep all receipts of income and expenses from the date of income tax collection and set up a diary book to record each day's transactions, separating debits and credits. Anyone with basic bookkeeping knowledge can do this. Other books can be temporarily not established. Furthermore, I believe that the income tax collection agency should adopt the continental system for account books, which is a point that can be researched. As stipulated by countries such as France and Italy, the journalized diary book is the statutory account book, and other original books are auxiliary journals. This is mostly the case with our country's existing accounting system, which can save the labor of changing. It can also be more systematic when auditing accounts.

A Woman Commits Suicide by Poison at the Yangtze Hotel 91

At the Yangtze Hotel at the intersection of Hankou Road and Yunnan Road, a young woman checked in the night before last. She claimed to be Wang Baozhen, 20 years old, from Shanghai, and requested room number 70 for her stay. Unexpectedly, around 6 a.m. yesterday, the tea server on the floor suddenly discovered that the woman had committed suicide by poison in the room. He immediately reported it to the police station, and they rushed her to the hospital for treatment. Because the throat wound was too severe, she was still unable to speak after regaining consciousness. Afterwards, police detectives found two suicide notes and a bottle of liquid in her room. They are currently searching for and notifying her family.

One Rain Makes It Autumn, Summer Scenery Has Faded 92

Clouds linger, the weather is cool and pleasant; a new hurricane is about to disturb Fujian and Guangdong.

Since the beginning of autumn on the eighth of this month, the climate in this city has been hot and humid, even more so than during the hottest days of summer. The temperature at noon often reaches 96 or 97 degrees, giving residents throughout the city the feeling of being in a furnace. However, the night before last (the 14th), there was a torrential downpour, and the heat immediately dissipated after the rain. Yesterday, it became even cooler and more pleasant. The highest temperature at noon was 90.05 degrees, and the sky was filled with lingering clouds, making it feel very unstable. According to reporters' inquiries at various epidemic hospitals, summer epidemics have greatly decreased. Sales of cold drinks in the market have also greatly decreased. The summer scenery is gradually fading away, and there is truly an atmosphere of one rain making it autumn. The first hurricane that arose in the Pacific Ocean has diminished after moving west through the Guangzhou Bay. According to the observatory's report at 2 p.m. yesterday, the second hurricane that newly arose in Peleliu Island has reached between 20 degrees north latitude and 119 degrees east longitude. The center of the hurricane is within 60 nautical miles of the reported direction, heading northwest by west, with very strong winds. If the direction does not change, there is a possibility of it disturbing the sea off Fujian and Guangdong.

The All-City Shantytown United Association is Established; Tang Anping and Twenty-Nine Others are Elected as Executive Committee Members; A Declaration is Issued Requesting Sympathy and Guidance from All Sectors 94

The New News Agency reports that the shantytown residents of the Pudong and Puxi districts of this city held the inaugural meeting of the All-City Shantytown United Association at the Ningbo Native Place Association on Xizang Road at 2 p.m. yesterday. Twenty-nine executive committee members were elected, and many important motions were resolved. A declaration was issued to announce to all sectors, and the Municipal Federation Association was temporarily borrowed as the office of the general association. They will start working immediately. Details are listed below.

Representatives Attending

Those who attended yesterday included representatives of the shantytowns on Yanshan Road, Chaoyang Road, Huishan Road, Lan Road, Qiwupu Road, Linping Road in the Pudong district, and Tokyo Road, Changping Road, Mabal Road, Putuo Road, Haifang Road, Guanchang Road, etc. in the Puxi district: Jia Zidong, Tang Anping, Xu Xiyuan, Zhang Sheyun, Sun Xudan, Zhu Jinsheng, Zhang Ziying, Wang Guiwen, and Chen Jiufeng, a representative of the First Special District Citizen United Association, as well as Ye Qichang, Pan Zhenxiang, and others from various district branches, totaling over 500 people. Zhu Qitai, Tang Anping, and Hu Yumen were publicly elected as the presidium of the meeting, and Zhang Zhiseng recorded.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony was performed, Chairman Tang Anping first gave a report, briefly stating: "Today, we are holding the inaugural meeting of the Shantytown United Association. We are very honored by your presence. At this time of industrial and commercial decline and economic depression, driven by the need for survival, we can only build shacks to barely shelter ourselves from the wind and rain. Now, the Municipal Council is not understanding our suffering and has ordered us to tear them down. If this is implemented, we will become homeless. Therefore, we have braved the dangers to appeal and petition, and fortunately, we have received sympathy and assistance from all sectors. Today's inaugural meeting is to show our success in uniting. We hope that you will uphold the current spirit and continue to work hard to achieve our goal of unity and common welfare." Hu Yumen then continued to report on the actual situation in the Puxi district, and the long speech is omitted.

Representatives' Speeches

Chen Jiufeng, representative of the First Special District Citizen United Association, said: "Today, your association is holding its inaugural meeting, and I, as a representative of the Citizen Association, am very honored to participate in this grand event. I am very pleased to see so many representatives attending today, with such enthusiasm. The Western philosopher said, 'The greater the oppression, the greater the resistance.' Today's situation is enough to prove that the Municipal Council, in the name of tidying up the city appearance, is ordering demolition without considering the lives of shantytown residents. Moreover, tidying up the city appearance should start with the downtown area. Look at the decline of Nanjing Road, but the Municipal Council is not trying to restore its prosperity. It can be seen that the Municipal Council's handling is not appropriate. Furthermore, tidying up the city appearance must also take into account the lives of ordinary people and should start from the root. The shantytown residents build shacks entirely because they are unable to afford the expensive rents, so they use them to avoid the wind and rain. Now that the United Association is established, it is to reasonably argue with the Municipal Council under a common and unified goal and request exemption from demolition. If they only issue strict demolition orders, resistance will be unavoidable. Therefore, the Citizen Association has repeatedly sent letters to the Municipal Council suggesting building affordable housing to settle the shantytown residents and to tidy the city. As for your association collecting membership fees, some people have reported it. However, I hope that you staff members will understand your own positions, be honest and self-respecting, and work hard for the public good. In terms of expenses, you should strive to save money and not leave room for criticism. As for saboteurs, you should thoroughly investigate them and punish them to warn the malicious. Furthermore, public training is currently being held. All shantytown residents are sound citizens, so they should all participate together and not fail in their national duties. After the United Association is established, it is hoped that you will gradually carry out negotiations on the exemption of shantytowns from demolition, promotion of hygiene work, and running literacy schools, etc., to achieve the goal of common welfare."

Motions Resolved

(1) Request the Municipal Council to exempt shantytowns from demolition: (Resolved) (A) In the name of the association, send a letter to the Municipal Council requesting consideration of the difficulties in the lives of ordinary people and granting exemption from demolition for existing shantytowns. (B) Issue a declaration requesting consistent assistance from all sectors. (C) Send a letter to the Taxpayers Association and the Citizen Association requesting that they continue to reasonably argue. (2) Request the Municipal Council to build affordable housing as soon as possible: (Resolved) Request the Municipal Council to allocate funds to do so, in order to gradually reduce shantytowns. (3) Conduct autonomous training in stages: (Resolved) (A) Have each group re-register the population and implement shantytown autonomy. (B) Have all shantytown residents take a citizenship oath. (C) Join the Citizen Association's citizenship training and request the establishment of shantytown training centers in Pudong and Puxi. (4) Automatically launch hygiene movement: (Resolved) (A) Hold hygiene exhibitions and hygiene lecture teams in stages in the Pudong and Puxi districts. (B) Clean up ditches and drill artesian wells. (5) Conduct literacy schools in stages: (Resolved) (A) Hold literacy lectures and performances. (B) Entrust the executive committee to establish literacy primary schools and after-school literacy night schools separately. (6) Conduct affordable clinics in stages: (Resolved) Entrust the executive committee to contact doctors and pharmacies near the shantytowns and establish affordable clinics for free consultation and medicine.

Election of Executive Committee

The meeting elected twenty-nine executive committee members. The list is as follows: Wang Qitai, Ji Yunsheng, Jia Zidong, Tang Anping, Xu Xiyuan, Zhang Buyun, Cheng Jingcheng, Qin Wenzhi, Yang Jinchen, Shen Qikuan, Xue Jian, Ding Jicong, Sun Xudan, Zhu Jinsheng, Zhang Ziying, Yin Yifu, Ruan Bukuan, Jiang Shanchang, Hu Yumen, Sun Weijin, Chen Jingqing, Xu Yifeng, Huang Yuzhang, Yao Shanfu, Wang Guiwen, Wang Chengguang, Tian Ruishan, Zhu Bohua, Yao Ziying, etc. The election ended and the meeting adjourned at 5 p.m.

Issuing a Declaration

The association issued a declaration yesterday, stating: "Because of the establishment of the United Association, the shantytown residents throughout the city will help each other in times of trouble, and the unity will be further consolidated. Our initiation of the United Association has two purposes: negative and positive. On the negative side, we do not avoid saying that we want to solve a kind of unreasonable oppression from external forces. On the positive side, we want to practice autonomy, self-improvement, and ceaseless effort to be a member who benefits society and the country. To the best of our ability, we will first conduct literacy education and hygiene movements, in order to eliminate illiteracy and strengthen physical fitness, and to establish joint security to reduce the authorities' concerns about public order. In short, we strive to be progressive, but our knowledge is limited, and our abilities are limited. We still hope that compatriots from all walks of life will give us sympathy and guidance."

Group of Thieves Conferring at 57 Xietu Road 95

Ximen Detective Team Arrests Three

Around 9 p.m. the night before last, Liu Guangjun, captain of the Ximen Sub-bureau's detective team, received a secret report from an informant stating that a large group of bandits were secretly conferring at Wang Xuezheng's house on the rear floor of 570 Xietu Road in the Nanshi area, planning to set off to rob somewhere. He immediately led team leaders Yu Ruhai, detectives Chen Miantong, Huang Shouxin, Chen Mingsheng, and other detectives, all disguised, and accompanied the informant to the house. They first surrounded the house on all sides and then rushed into the house. Just as the thieves finished their meeting and were coming downstairs, they were able to arrest Wang Wanlong (33 years old) from Taizhou, Zhu Youming (29 years old), Wang Jiagui (30 years old), and three others. A revolver and two bullets were found on Zhu. They then led the team to interrogate them separately. According to the thieves, they were discussing setting off to rob the Tongxing Sock Factory on Liyuan Road and the North China Transportation Company within two days, where there were 2,000 yuan in wages to be robbed. They then confessed that their fellow villager Shi Liuba, 27 years old, worked as a barber in the North China Transportation Company. The detectives then led the thieves to a thatched shed at the North China Transportation wharf overnight and captured Shi Liuba. Yesterday morning, they interrogated the suspects again and they also confessed that on the 7th of last month, they had conspired to rob Chen Changsen, foreman of the China Cement Company at 1 Xijichang West Road in Caohejing, of 160 yuan, and had often hit Chen in the head with a gun butt. This was arranged by Er Mazi, who set up the robbery on the road. Captain Liu verified the confessions. As the case involved conspiracy to rob, he sent the four suspects along with the gun and bullets to the Ximen Sub-bureau. Chief Yao briefly questioned them and, because the case was important, ordered that a document be prepared and submitted to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for questioning.

High Tide Starting Last Night on the Huangpu River for Three Days 96

Only Inches Away From the Bund Embankment; Tide Water May Overflow the Bank; Yong'an's Side Road Is Filled Higher

According to the Huangpu Conservancy Bureau's prediction, the highest tide levels on the Huangpu River since the 13th of this month will be the night tides of the past, present and next three days, which are very close to the embankments. The details are recorded below:

High Tide Starting Yesterday

According to the Huangpu Conservancy Bureau's prediction, the high tide level on the Huangpu River at 11:45 p.m. on the 16th was 12 feet 6.5 inches. At 12:18 a.m. on the 17th, the high tide level was 12 feet 5.4 inches. At 12:51 a.m. on the 18th, the high tide level was 12 feet 8 inches. The Bund embankment is 13 feet high, and the water level is only four inches to two inches away from the embankment. Therefore, not only will the low-lying roads be flooded, but there is also the possibility of water overflowing the embankment at the low points, which should be noted.

Low Road Filled Higher

The especially low section of the road on the side of the Wing On Company at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Zhejiang Road has always been flooded during high tide periods, causing water accumulation and greatly hindering traffic. Therefore, the Municipal Council specially sent workers to fill the road surface by two feet last month. The same was done on the section of Jiujiang Road from Hubei Road in the east to Zhejiang Road in the west. This project has now been completed. It is reported that the Engineering Department will also fill other especially low roads.

The Chinese Buddhist Association Earnestly Exercises its Powers and Supervises the Management of Temple Property 98

The Chinese Buddhist Association believes that the Buddhist associations at all levels throughout the country are religious organizations. According to the association's constitution, they naturally have considerable responsibility and authority for the enforcement of religious rules, the propagation of religious doctrines, the handling of charitable and public welfare matters, and the supervision and management of temple property. However, some local governments mistakenly believe that the Buddhist association is a cultural organization and only order it to study religious doctrines, not allowing it to inquire about the temple property that has been occupied or to organize various religious affairs. It has specially submitted a request to the Ministry of Interior to order the civil affairs departments of all provinces to inform their subordinates to take note of this. It is reported that the association has now received an approval from the Ministry of Interior to issue a notice.

Recent News on the Li Society Art Exhibition 99

The "Li Society Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition" held by famous calligraphers and painters from Beijing and Shanghai has been open for nine days, and more than 40,000 guests have visited. Today, it has been re-displayed with the addition of new works. These include "Landscape" by Ms. Wang Changbao, the eldest daughter of Wang Jingqi, the newly appointed minister to Sweden and Norway, "Figures" by Ms. Zhang Manjun, wife of Li Gongpu, "Buddhist Images" by Wang Yiting, "Pine and Crane" by Zhang Yuguang, "Tiger, Lotus, Flowers and Birds" by Hu Zaobin, "Flowers" by Zhang Shuqi, "Buddhist Images" by Qian Huafo, "Plum and Pine" by Zhang Xiaolou, "Landscape" by Yuan Songnian, "Flowers and Birds" by Lin Jieru, "Animals" by Xu Beihong, "Tiger" by Xiong Songquan, and "Flowers and Birds" by Hong Shuan, totaling more than 100 pieces. Today's guests were mostly British, Japanese, American, and people from this country, who all praised the greatness of the Li Society and lingered, reluctant to leave. Many books were purchased, and some even came to visit for several days, which proves the depth of Chinese art. There are only three days left before the closing, so those who love calligraphy and painting should not miss this good opportunity.

Further Trial of the Assault Case: Feng Kaizhu's Condition Critical; Sent to Forensic Doctor for Examination of Injuries; Li Jiusheng to be Tried Indefinitely 103

Li Jiusheng, from Jiangxi, was walking near Liaoyang Road, Tangshan Road, at 7:35 PM on the 5th of this month, when Meng Zhaohua and Meng Zhaogui, brothers from Taixing, were enjoying the cool air there. They were carelessly catching dragonflies, and the bamboo pole accidentally struck Li's head, leading to a dispute. Subsequently, both sides called upon dozens of fellow townsmen, wielding iron rods and spears, resulting in a brawl. As a result, Feng Kaizhu, a thug from the Taixing gang, was stabbed in the chest with a spear by the Jiangxi side and fell to the ground, barely breathing. Yu Lin Road Police Station's Western Detective, Mr. Whithower, Detective Li Hongsheng, and Chinese Constables No. 2018 and No. 1364 rushed to the scene upon hearing the alarm, arrested Li, and collected three spears from the ground, taking them all to the police station and transferring them to the First Special District Court. Because the victim was in St. Luke's Hospital, his injuries were severe, and he was unable to testify in court, so it was decided to postpone the trial, and the defendant Li was remanded in custody. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xiefen arrived at the Third Criminal Court for a continuation of the trial. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu, of the Municipal Council, stated that the victim, Deng Kaizhu, had been unconscious since entering the hospital and had not spoken a word to this day. According to the doctor, there was no immediate danger to his life, and he would recover in two weeks. He was carried to the courtroom on a bed. The court ordered him to be brought inside to be questioned, but he still did not speak. He was ordered to be sent to the forensic doctor's office to examine the injuries to determine if there were any dangerous changes. Li Jiusheng was remanded in custody pending an indefinite trial.

News of the Xu-Pan Litigation 109

Xu Bozhang, from Minhou, Fujian, 40 years old, has been engaged in the glass factory business in Shanghai for many years. In the tenth year of the Republic [1921], he married Wang Aiyu (35 years old this year) in his hometown and lived in the countryside. Because Xu was doing business in Shanghai, he was not accustomed to sleeping alone. On September 14, 1934, through the introduction of friends Yang Zhifang and Wang Shuying, he married Pan Jingyu (21 years old this year), a woman from Changzhou, as his wife. After their wedding at the Oriental Hotel, they rented a house and lived together at No. 50, Fengyu Lane, Rue Saussier in the French Concession. In October of the following year, a daughter was born, named Dezhen. However, when Xu married Pan, he did not mention his wife in his hometown. In mid-March of this year, Xu's wife, Wang Aiyu, came to Shanghai from Fujian. Xu rented Room 22 of the Dacheng Apartments on Rue Paul Beau and lived with Wang. His feelings for Pan gradually faded from then on, and he cut off her living expenses. Pan found out that Xu had a new lover and was living with her outside. After discovering their address, she was unwilling to accept it. Therefore, on April 1, Pan reported to the French police station that her husband was committing adultery with someone in the apartment. Detectives were dispatched to Dacheng Apartments and arrested Xu and Wang Aiyu. After the police chief learned that they were a legally married couple, no public prosecution was initiated. Pan Jingyu then accused Xu Bozhang of bigamy and abandonment. The police station sent Xu to the Second Special District Court for prosecution according to the law. After Judge Li Changnian's trial, he believed that the statute of limitations had passed and did not convict him. After Xu was released, Wang Aiyu independently hired a lawyer and filed a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court, accusing Pan Jingyu of obstructing freedom and defamation, and attached a civil lawsuit seeking 1,000 yuan in damages for mental and reputational losses. Judge Li Changnian also summoned both parties for trial. The result of the trial was that the fault lay with Xu Bozhang, and there was no reason for the plaintiff's claims. Pan Jingyu was found not guilty. Wang Aiyu refused to accept the judgment and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the High Court. On the morning of the day before yesterday, Judge Liao of the High Court arrived at the Second Criminal Court to investigate and question the appellant and the appellee. Both were accompanied by lawyers. After the court questioned them, and the two sides stated the circumstances of the case, the court ordered the hearing to be postponed to the morning of the 29th. However, after Pan Jingyu's criminal case against Xu Bozhang failed, she filed a lawsuit in the Civil Court for damages for support. Because Xu's whereabouts were unknown, the case was still pending.

Young Photographic Reporter Chen Jiazhen Passed Away Yesterday Morning 117

The young photographic reporter Chen Jiazhen had an extremely detached style and a very fresh perspective. Therefore, his works were extremely welcomed by society. However, due to accumulated overwork, he fell ill and sought medical treatment repeatedly, but it was ineffective. This was when the rumors that Chen had disappeared began to circulate. At the beginning of this month, Chen's friends, including Lin Zecang, transferred him from the Taijia Hospital to the Tuberculosis Isolation and Treatment Department of the Hongqiao Sanitarium in West Shanghai. After diagnosis by the hospital's doctors using X-rays, it was determined that he had caseous pneumonia of both lungs and was diagnosed as incurable. After admission, the treatment process was very good. Chen's friends hoped that he would recover without medication. However, he eventually died of heart failure and exhaustion at 5:10 AM yesterday. The world of photography has lost another talent. The remains were sent to the Shanghai Funeral Home for embalming. According to the attending physician at the hospital, Chen's lung disease was discovered too late, and he lost the opportunity for proper treatment. After it was discovered, he took too much medicine, hoping for a lucky recovery, which delayed the time and the disease became incurable. This is a formula for the rampant spread of lung disease in our country. Chen was such a talented young man, and yet this happened. How many such tragedies are staged every year among the general public with no common sense? The only way to remedy this is to promote X-rays, early diagnosis, and detect this type of asymptomatic tuberculosis, and then apply proper treatment. Sixty-seven to eighty-five percent of cases can be expected to be cured and their lives saved. However, this proper treatment is quite interesting in our country's situation. According to research by experts from various countries, the first thing to do is to abandon superstitious prescriptions, which are regarded by patients in our country as life-saving medicine. The second thing to understand is that in addition to the four major supplementary therapies of sunlight, air, rest, and nutrition, there is also a more reliable surgical treatment, which can not only shorten the treatment time, save the patient's economy, eradicate the root cause of the disease, and reduce the risk of infection, directly improving personal health and family happiness, but also indirectly contributing to social construction and national productivity. In short, the reason why there are so many lung diseases in our country is that too many people believe in medicine. If the life of each patient is extended by one to three years, the total amount of medical expenses, calculated nationwide, will be greater than the cost of any national construction project. The reason why lung diseases have decreased in various countries, such as in the United States, where lung disease has decreased from the leading cause of death to the seventh, is due to the popularization of this proper treatment.

Ye Gongchuo Requests Preservation of the Ming Dynasty Zhengtong Edition of the Buddhist Canon: Shipped from Ruifan Temple in Pixian County to Shanghai for Storage at the Local Buddhist Artifact Preservation Museum 119

According to Datong News Agency, Ye Gongchuo, the director of the Shanghai Buddhist Artifact Preservation Museum at No. 418, Hart Road, requested that the Ming Dynasty Zhengtong edition of the Buddhist canon stored in Ruixiang Temple on Mount Suyang in Pixian County be transported to Shanghai for preservation at the museum to avoid desecration. He sent a letter to the Buddhist Association of China stating that the Ruixiang Temple on Mount Suyang in Pixian County has a collection of the Ming Dynasty Zhengtong edition of the Buddhist canon. Due to poor management in recent years, much of it has been lost. There are currently 2,935 volumes of Sanskrit text and 338 volumes of Qian text. If no measures are taken to preserve it, this Buddhist scripture will inevitably be lost, which is a great pity. Our museum, for the purpose of preserving Buddhist artifacts, intends to find a way to transport it to Shanghai for proper preservation. We have reached an agreement with the abbot of the temple and have consulted with the Pixian County Government to temporarily store the scriptures in the government office. Accordingly, we are writing to your association for approval, and we ask that you inform the Pixian County Government to investigate. Please pack and seal all the books and transport them to our museum at No. 418, Hart Road, Shanghai. Our museum will be responsible for reimbursing all transportation costs. The association has forwarded a letter to the Pixian County Government to have all of the scriptures transported to Shanghai for preservation.
